text-decoration: none; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); box-sizing: border-box; border-bottom: 1px dotted rgb(0, 0, 0);">Apache CouchDB</a></span></span></b><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"><span style="font-family: proxima-nova, sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 16px;"><b>, like Redis, Cassandra, and MongoDB, is a <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">NoSQL database</em></b>. CouchDB stores data as JSON documents which are non-relational in nature. This allows users of CouchDB to store data in ways that look very similar to their real world counterparts.</span></span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: proxima-nova, sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"><br/></span></span></span></div></div></div><div style="font-family:gotham, helvetica, arial, sans-serif;font-size:14px;"><div style="position: relative; text-align: left;"><strong style="font-family: &quot;lucida grande&quot;, helvetica, arial, san-serif;">Gnuplot and GLPK:</strong></td><td style="font-family: &quot;lucida grande&quot;, helvetica, arial, san-serif; text-align: left;"><a href="http://hyperpolyglot.org/misc-math" style="font-family: &quot;lucida grande&quot;, helvetica, arial, san-serif; color: rgb(0, 0, 170); transition: background-color 0.3s ease;">Gnuplot, GLPK</a></td></tr><tr style="font-family: &quot;lucida grande&quot;, helvetica, arial, san-serif;"><td style="font-family: &quot;lucida grande&quot;, helvetica, arial, san-serif; text-align: left;"><strong style="font-family: &quot;lucida grande&quot;, helvetica, arial, san-serif;">Fortran and APL:</strong></td><td style="font-family: &quot;lucida grande&quot;, helvetica, arial, san-serif; text-align: left;"><strong style="font-family: &quot;lucida grande&quot;, helvetica, arial, san-serif;">Relational Data and JSON Tools:</strong></td><td style="font-family: &quot;lucida grande&quot;, helvetica, arial, san-serif; text-align: left;"><a href="http://hyperpolyglot.org/data" style="font-family: &quot;lucida grande&quot;, helvetica, arial, san-serif; color: rgb(0, 0, 170); transition: background-color 0.3s ease;">SQL, Awk, Pig</a>, <a href="http://hyperpolyglot.org/json" style="font-family: &quot;lucida grande&quot;, helvetica, arial, san-serif; color: rgb(0, 0, 170); transition: background-color 0.3s ease;">Jq</a></td></tr><tr style="font-family: &quot;lucida grande&quot;, helvetica, arial, san-serif;"><td style="font-family: &quot;lucida grande&quot;, helvetica, arial, san-serif; text-align: left;"><a href="http://hyperpolyglot.org/lightweight-markup" style="font-family: &quot;lucida grande&quot;, helvetica, arial, san-serif; color: rgb(0, 0, 170); transition: background-color 0.3s ease;">Markdown, reStructuredText, MediaWiki, AsciiDoc, Org-mode</a></td></tr><tr style="font-family: &quot;lucida grande&quot;, helvetica, arial, san-serif;"><td style="font-family: &quot;lucida grande&quot;, helvetica, arial, san-serif; text-align: left;"><strong style="font-family: &qquot;lucida grande&quot;, helvetica, arial, san-serif;">2D Vector Graphics:</strong></td><td style="font-family: &quot;lucida grande&quot;, helvetica, arial, san-serif; text-align: left;"><a href="http://hyperpolyglot.org/vector-graphics" style="font-family: &quot;lucida grande&quot;, helvetica, arial, san-serif; color: rgb(0, 0, 170); transition: background-color 0.3s ease;">PostScript, Processing, SVG</a></td></tr></tbody></table></div></div></div></div><div><div style="font-family:&quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Arial, sans;font-size:16px;"><span style="color: rgb(36, 39, 41);"><span style="font-size: 15px;"><span style="font-family: Arial, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, sans-serif;"><b><br/></b></span></span></span></div></div><div style="font-family:gotham, helvetica, arial, sans-serif;font-size:14px;"><br/></div><div><hr/></div><div><span style="color: rgb(36, 39, 41);"><span style="font-size: 15px;"><span style="font-family: Arial, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, sans-serif;"><b>Map vs Dictionary vs Associative Array vs Hash Map = SAME FUCKING THING</b></span></span></span></div><div><span style="color: rgb(36, 39, 41);"><span style="font-size: 15px;"><span style="font-family: Arial, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, sans-serif;">Two terms for the same thing</span></span></span></div></div><p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-size: 15px; clear: both; color: rgb(36, 39, 41); font-family: Arial, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><em style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-size: 15px; font-style: italic;">&quot;Map&quot;</em> is used by Java, C++<br/><em style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-size: 15px; font-style: italic;">&quot;Dictionary&quot;</em> is used by .Net, Python<br/><em style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-size: 15px; font-style: italic;">&quot;Associative array&quot;</em> is used by Javascript, PHP</p><div style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-size: 15px; clear: both; color: rgb(36, 39, 41); font-family: Arial, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div><em style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-size: 15px; font-style: italic;">&quot;Map&quot;</em> is the correct mathematical term, but it is avoided because it has separate meaning in <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Map_%28higher-order_function%29" style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-size: 15px; color: rgb(0, 89, 153); text-decoration: none; cursor: pointer;">functional programming</a>.</div></div></div><div><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div><span style="font-family: sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);">In </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Computer_science" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Computer science">computer science</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);">, an <b>associative array</b>, <b>map</b>, <b>symbol table</b>, or <b>dictionary</b> is an </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Abstract_data_type" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Abstract data type">abstract data type</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"> composed of a </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Collection_(computing)" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Collection (computing)">collection</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"> of </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Attribute%E2%80%93value_pair" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Attribute–value pair">(key, value)</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"> pairs, such that each possible key appears at most once in the collection.</span></span></div></div></div><div><span style="font-family: sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"><br/></span></span></div><div><hr/></div><div><span style="font-family: sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);">In </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mathematics" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Mathematics">mathematics</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"> and </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Computer_science" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Computer science">computer science</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);">, <b>currying</b> is the technique of translating the evaluation of a </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Function_(mathematics)" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Function (mathematics)">function</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"> that takes multiple </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Parameter_(computer_science)" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Parameter (computer science)">arguments</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"> (or a </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tuple" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Tuple">tuple</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"> of arguments) into evaluating a sequence of functions, each with a single argument. Currying is related to, but not the same as, </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Partial_application" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Partial application">partial application</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);">.</span></span></div></div></div><div><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; color: rgb(37, 37, 37); font-family: sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div><br/></div><div><hr/></div><div>In <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language_theory" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Programming language theory">programming language theory</a>, <b>lazy evaluation</b>, or <b>call-by-need</b><sup style="unicode-bidi: isolate; white-space: nowrap; font-size: 11.2px; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal;"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lazy_evaluation#cite_note-1" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none; white-space: nowrap;">[1]</a></sup> is an <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Evaluation_strategy" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Evaluation strategy">evaluation strategy</a> which delays the evaluation of an <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Expression_(computer_science)" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Expression (computer science)">expression</a> until its value is needed (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Non-strict_evaluation" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Non-strict evaluation">non-strict evaluation</a>) and which also avoids repeated evaluations (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sharing_(computer_science)" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Sharing (computer science)">sharing</a>).<sup style="unicode-bidi: isolate; white-space: nowrap; font-size: 11.2px; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal;"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lazy_evaluation#cite_note-WattFindlay2004-2" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none; white-space: nowrap;">[2]</a></sup><sup style="unicode-bidi: isolate; white-space: nowrap; font-size: 11.2px; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal;"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lazy_evaluation#cite_note-3" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none; white-space: nowrap;">[3]</a></sup> The sharing can reduce the running time of certain functions by an exponential factor over other non-strict evaluation strategies, such as <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Call-by-name" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Call-by-name">call-by-name</a>.<sup style="font-size: 11.2px; white-space: nowrap;">[<i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (March 2011)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup></div></div></div><div><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"><span style="font-family: sans-serif;"><br/></span></span></div><div><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; color: rgb(37, 37, 37); font-family: sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div><hr/></div><div>In <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Computer_science" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Computer science">computer science</a>, <b>pattern matching</b> is the act of checking a given <b>sequence</b> of tokens for the presence of the constituents of some <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pattern" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Pattern">pattern</a>. In contrast to <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pattern_recognition" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Pattern recognition">pattern recognition</a>, the match usually has to be exact. The patterns generally have the form of either <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/String_(computer_science)" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="String (computer science)">sequences</a> or <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tree_structure" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Tree structure">tree structures</a>. Uses of pattern matching include outputting the locations (if any) of a pattern within a token sequence, to output some component of the matched pattern, and to substitute the matching pattern with some other token sequence (i.e., <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Regular_expression" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Regular expression">search and replace</a>).</div></div></div><div><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; color: rgb(37, 37, 37); font-family: sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div><br/></div><div><hr/></div><div>In <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Computer_programming" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Computer programming">computer programming</a>, more so <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Functional_programming" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Functional programming">functional programming</a> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Type_theory" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Type theory">type theory</a>, an <b>algebraic data type</b> is a kind of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Composite_type" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Composite type">composite type</a>, i.e., a type formed by combining other types.</div></div><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-family: sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);">Two common classes of algebraic types are </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Product_type" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Product type">product types</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"> (i.e., </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tuple" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Tuple">tuples</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"> and </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Record_(computer_science)" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Record (computer science)">records</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);">) and </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sum_type" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Sum type">sum types</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);">, also called tagged or disjoint unions or <i>variant types</i>.<sup style="unicode-bidi: isolate; white-space: nowrap; font-size: 11.2px; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal;"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Algebraic_data_type#cite_note-1" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none; white-space: nowrap;">[1]</a></sup></span></div></div></div><div><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div><span style="font-family: sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"><br/></span></span></div><div><hr/></div><div><p style="margin: 0.5em 0px; color: rgb(37, 37, 37); font-family: sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">In <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Computer_science" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Computer science">computer science</a>, <b>syntactic sugar</b> is <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Syntax_(programming_languages)" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Syntax (programming languages)">syntax</a> within a <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Programming language">programming language</a> that is designed to make things easier to read or to express. It makes the language &quot;sweeter&quot; for human use: things can be expressed more clearly, more concisely, or in an alternative style that some may prefer.</p><p style="margin: 0.5em 0px; color: rgb(37, 37, 37); font-family: sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">For example, many programming languages provide special syntax for referencing and updating <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Array_data_type" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Array data type">array</a> elements. Abstractly, an array reference is a procedure of two arguments: an array and a subscript vector, which could be expressed as <code style="font-family: monospace, Courier; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: rgb(248, 249, 250); border: 1px solid rgb(234, 236, 240); border-radius: 2px; padding: 1px 4px;">get_array(Array, vector(i,j))</code>. Instead, many languages provide syntax like <code style="font-family: monospace, Courier; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: rgb(248, 249, 250); border: 1px solid rgb(234, 236, 240); border-radius: 2px; padding: 1px 4px;">Array[i,j]</code>. Similarly an array element update is a procedure of three arguments, something like <code style="font-family: monospace, Courier; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: rgb(248, 249, 250); border: 1px solid rgb(234, 236, 240); border-radius: 2px; padding: 1px 4px;">set_array(Array, vector(i,j), value)</code>, but many languages provide syntax like <code style="font-family: monospace, Courier; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: rgb(248, 249, 250); border: 1px solid rgb(234, 236, 240); border-radius: 2px; padding: 1px 4px;">Array[i,j] = value</code>.</p></div><div><br/></div><div><hr/></div><div><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"><span style="font-family: sans-serif;">In programming, <b>operator overloading</b>, sometimes termed <i>operator <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ad_hoc_polymorphism" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Ad hoc polymorphism">ad hoc polymorphism</a></i>, is a specific case of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polymorphism_(computer_science)" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Polymorphism (computer science)">polymorphism</a>, where different <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Operator_(programming)" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Operator (programming)">operators</a> have different implementations depending on their arguments. Operator overloading is generally defined by a <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Programming language">programming language</a>, a <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programmer" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Programmer">programmer</a>, or both.</span></span></div><div><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"><span style="font-family: sans-serif;"><br/></span></span></div><div><p style="margin: 0.5em 0px; color: rgb(37, 37, 37); font-family: sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">Operator overloading is <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Syntactic_sugar" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Syntactic sugar">syntactic sugar</a>, and is used because it allows programming using notation nearer to the target domain<sup style="unicode-bidi: isolate; white-space: nowrap; font-size: 11.2px; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal;"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Operator_overloading#cite_note-1" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none; white-space: nowrap;">[1]</a></sup> and allows user-defined types a similar level of syntactic support as types built into a language. It is common, for example, in scientific computing, where it allows computing representations of mathematical objects to be manipulated with the same syntax as on paper.</p><p style="margin: 0.5em 0px; color: rgb(37, 37, 37); font-family: sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">Operator overloading does not change the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Expressive_power_(computer_science)" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Expressive power (computer science)">expressive power</a> of a language (with functions), as it can be emulated using function calls. For example, consider variables <code style="font-family: monospace, Courier; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: rgb(248, 249, 250); border: 1px solid rgb(234, 236, 240); border-radius: 2px; padding: 1px 4px;">a, b, c</code> of some user-defined type, such as <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Matrix_(mathematics)" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Matrix (mathematics)">matrices</a>:</p><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div><code style="font-family: monospace, Courier; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: rgb(248, 249, 250); border: 1px solid rgb(234, 236, 240); border-radius: 2px; padding: 1px 4px;">a + b * c</code></div><div><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"><span style="font-family: monospace, Courier;"><span style="background-color: rgb(248, 249, 250);"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"><br/></span></span></span></span></div><div><hr/></div><div><h2 style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background: none rgb(255, 255, 255); font-weight: normal; margin: 1em 0px 0.25em; overflow: hidden; padding: 0px; border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(162, 169, 177); font-size: 1.5em; font-family: &quot;Linux Libertine&quot;, Georgia, Times, serif; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;">Multiline string literals<span style="user-select: none; font-size: small; font-weight: normal; margin-left: 1em; vertical-align: baseline; display: inline-block; white-space: nowrap; unicode-bidi: isolate; font-family: sans-serif;"><span style="margin-right: 0.25em; color: rgb(85, 85, 85);">[</span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=String_literal&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Edit section: Multiline string literals">edit</a><span style="margin-left: 0.25em; color: rgb(85, 85, 85);">]</span></span></h2><p style="margin: 0.5em 0px; color: rgb(37, 37, 37); font-family: sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">In many languages, string literals can contain literal newlines, spanning several lines. Alternatively, newlines can be escaped, most often as <code style="font-family: monospace, Courier; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: rgb(248, 249, 250); border: 1px solid rgb(234, 236, 240); border-radius: 2px; padding: 1px 4px;">\n</code>. For example:</p><div dir="ltr" style="background: rgb(248, 248, 248); direction: ltr; unicode-bidi: embed; color: rgb(37, 37, 37); font-family: sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;"><pre style="font-family: monospace, Courier; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: rgb(248, 249, 250); border: 1px solid rgb(234, 236, 240); padding: 1em; white-space: pre-wrap; tab-size: 4;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 128, 0);">echo</span> <span style="color: rgb(186, 33, 33);">'foo</span>
<span style="color: rgb(186, 33, 33);">bar'</span>
</pre></div><p style="margin: 0.5em 0px; color: rgb(37, 37, 37); font-family: sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">and</p><div dir="ltr" style="background: rgb(248, 248, 248); direction: ltr; unicode-bidi: embed; color: rgb(37, 37, 37); font-family: sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;"><div style="font-family: monospace, Courier; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: rgb(248, 249, 250); border: 1px solid rgb(234, 236, 240); padding: 1em; tab-size: 4;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 128, 0);">echo</span> -e <span style="color: rgb(186, 33, 33);">&quot;foo\nbar&quot;</span></div></div></div></div></div></div><p style="margin: 0.5em 0px; color: rgb(37, 37, 37); font-family: sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"></p></div><div><b><span style="font-family: sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"><br/></span></span></b></div><div><hr/></div><div><p style="margin: 0.5em 0px; color: rgb(37, 37, 37); font-family: sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">In <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Object-oriented_programming" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Object-oriented programming">object-oriented programming</a>, a <b>protocol</b> or <b>interface</b> is a common means for unrelated <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Object_(computer_science)" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Object (computer science)">objects</a> to communicate with each other. These are definitions of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Method_(computer_science)" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Method (computer science)">methods</a> and values which the objects agree upon in order to co-operate.<sup style="unicode-bidi: isolate; white-space: nowrap; font-size: 11.2px; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal;"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Protocol_(object-oriented_programming)#cite_note-1" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none; white-space: nowrap;">[1]</a></sup></p><p style="margin: 0.5em 0px; color: rgb(37, 37, 37); font-family: sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">For example, in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Java_(programming_language)" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Java (programming language)">Java</a> (where protocols are termed <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Interface_(Java)" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Interface (Java)">interfaces</a></i>), the <tt style="font-family: monospace, Courier;">Comparable</tt> interface specifies a method <tt style="font-family: monospace, Courier;">compareTo()</tt> which implementing classes should implement. This means that a separate sorting method, for example, can sort any object which implements the Comparable interface, without having to know anything about the inner nature of the class (except that two of these objects can be compared by means of <tt style="font-family: monospace, Courier;">compareTo()</tt>).</p></div><div><br/></div><div><hr/></div><div><h2 style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background: none rgb(255, 255, 255); font-weight: normal; margin: 1em 0px 0.25em; overflow: hidden; padding: 0px; border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(162, 169, 177); font-size: 1.5em; font-family: &quot;Linux Libertine&quot;, Georgia, Times, serif; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;">Exception handling in software<span style="user-select: none; font-size: small; font-weight: normal; margin-left: 1em; vertical-align: baseline; display: inline-block; white-space: nowrap; unicode-bidi: isolate; font-family: sans-serif;"><span style="margin-right: 0.25em; color: rgb(85, 85, 85);">[</span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Exception_handling&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Edit section: Exception handling in software">edit</a><span style="margin-left: 0.25em; color: rgb(85, 85, 85);">]</span></span></h2><p style="margin: 0.5em 0px; color: rgb(37, 37, 37); font-family: sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">Software exception handling and the support provided by software tools differs somewhat from what is understood under exception in hardware, but similar concepts are involved. In programming language mechanisms for exception handling, the term <i>exception</i> is typically used in a specific sense to denote a data structure storing information about an exceptional condition. One mechanism to transfer control, or <i>raise</i> an exception, is known as a <i>throw</i>. The exception is said to be <i>thrown</i>. Execution is transferred to a &quot;catch&quot;.</p></div><div><br/></div><div><hr/></div><div><span style="font-size: 24px;"><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"><span style="font-family: sans-serif;"><b>Go</b></span></span></span></div><div><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"><span style="font-family: sans-serif;">(often referred to as <b>golang</b>) is a <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Free_software" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Free software">free</a> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Open-source" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Open-source">open source</a><sup style="unicode-bidi: isolate; white-space: nowrap; font-size: 11.2px; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal;"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Go_(programming_language)#cite_note-12" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none; white-space: nowrap;">[12]</a></sup> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Programming language">programming language</a> created at <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Google" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Google">Google</a><sup style="unicode-bidi: isolate; white-space: nowrap; font-size: 11.2px; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal;"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Go_(programming_language)#cite_note-13" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none; white-space: nowrap;">[13]</a></sup> in 2007 by Robert Griesemer, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Rob_Pike" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Rob Pike">Rob Pike</a>, and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ken_Thompson" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Ken Thompson">Ken Thompson</a>.<sup style="unicode-bidi: isolate; white-space: nowrap; font-size: 11.2px; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal;"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Go_(programming_language)#cite_note-langfaq-10" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none; white-space: nowrap;">[10]</a></sup> It is a <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Compiler" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Compiler">compiled</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Static_typing" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Static typing">statically typed</a> language in the tradition of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ALGOL" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="ALGOL">Algol</a> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/C_(programming_language)" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="C (programming language)">C</a>, with <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Garbage_collection_(computer_science)" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Garbage collection (computer science)">garbage collection</a>, limited <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Structural_type_system" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Structural type system">structural typing</a>,<sup style="unicode-bidi: isolate; white-space: nowrap; font-size: 11.2px; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal;"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Go_(programming_language)#cite_note-structural_typing-3" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none; white-space: nowrap;">[3]</a></sup> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Memory_safety" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Memory safety">memory safety</a> features and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Communicating_sequential_processes" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Communicating sequential processes">CSP</a>-style <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Concurrent_programming" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Concurrent programming">concurrent programming</a> features added.<sup style="unicode-bidi: isolate; white-space: nowrap; font-size: 11.2px; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal;"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Go_(programming_language)#cite_note-boldly-14" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none; white-space: nowrap;">[14]</a></sup></span></span></div><div><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"><span style="font-family: sans-serif;"><sup><span style="font-size: 11.2px;"><br/></span></sup></span></span></div><div><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; color: rgb(37, 37, 37); font-family: sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div><span style="font-size: 24px;"><b>Dart</b></span> </div><div>is a <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/General-purpose_programming_language" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="General-purpose programming language">general-purpose programming language</a> originally developed by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Google" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Google">Google</a> and later approved as a standard by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ecma" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Ecma">Ecma</a> (ECMA-408).<sup style="unicode-bidi: isolate; white-space: nowrap; font-size: 11.2px; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal;"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dart_(programming_language)#cite_note-4" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none; white-space: nowrap;">[4]</a></sup> It is used to build web, server and mobile applications, and for <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Internet_of_Things" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Internet of Things">Internet of Things</a> (IoT) devices.<sup style="unicode-bidi: isolate; white-space: nowrap; font-size: 11.2px; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal;"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dart_(programming_language)#cite_note-5" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none; white-space: nowrap;">[5]</a></sup> It is <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Open-source_software" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Open-source software">open-source software</a> under a <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Permissive_free_software_license" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Permissive free software license">permissive free software license</a> (modified <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/BSD_licenses" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="BSD licenses">BSD license</a>).</div></div><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; color: rgb(37, 37, 37); font-family: sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div>Dart is an <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Object-oriented_programming" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Object-oriented programming">object-oriented</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Class-based_programming" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Class-based programming">class defined</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Single_inheritance" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Single inheritance">single inheritance</a> language using <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/C_Sharp_(programming_language)" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="C Sharp (programming language)">C#</a> style <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Syntax_(programming_languages)" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Syntax (programming languages)">syntax</a> that <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Transcompile" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Transcompile">transcompiles</a> optionally into <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/JavaScript" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="JavaScript">JavaScript</a>. It supports <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Interface_(object-oriented_programming)" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Interface (object-oriented programming)">interfaces</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mixin" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Mixin">mixins</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Abstract_class" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Abstract class">abstract classes</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Reification_(computer_science)" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Reification (computer science)">reified</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Generic_programming" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Generic programming">generics</a>, and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Optional_typing" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Optional typing">optional typing</a>.</div></div><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div><br/></div></div></div></div></div><div><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; color: rgb(37, 37, 37); font-family: sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div><span style="font-size: 24px;"><b>Lisp</b></span></div><div>(historically, <b>LISP</b>) is a family of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Computer" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Computer">computer</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Programming language">programming languages</a> with a long history and a distinctive, fully <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Parenthesized" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Parenthesized">parenthesized</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_notation#Computer_programming" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Polish notation">prefix notation</a>.<sup style="unicode-bidi: isolate; white-space: nowrap; font-size: 11.2px; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal;"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lisp_(programming_language)#cite_note-3" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none; white-space: nowrap;">[3]</a></sup> Originally specified in 1958, Lisp is the second-oldest <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/High-level_programming_language" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="High-level programming language">high-level programming language</a> in widespread use today. Only <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fortran" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Fortran">Fortran</a> is older, by one year.<sup style="unicode-bidi: isolate; white-space: nowrap; font-size: 11.2px; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal;"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lisp_(programming_language)#cite_note-4" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none; white-space: nowrap;">[4]</a></sup><sup style="unicode-bidi: isolate; white-space: nowrap; font-size: 11.2px; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal;"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lisp_(programming_language)#cite_note-5" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none; white-space: nowrap;">[5]</a></sup> Lisp has changed since its early days, and many <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language_dialect" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Programming language dialect">dialects</a> have existed over its history. Today, the best known general-purpose <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lisp_dialects" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Lisp dialects">Lisp dialects</a> are <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Common_Lisp" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Common Lisp">Common Lisp</a> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scheme_(programming_language)" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Scheme (programming language)">Scheme</a>.</div></div><p style="margin: 0.5em 0px; color: rgb(37, 37, 37); font-family: sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">Lisp was originally created as a practical <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mathematical_notation" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Mathematical notation">mathematical notation</a> for <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Computer_programs" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Computer programs">computer programs</a>, influenced by the notation of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Alonzo_Church" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Alonzo Church">Alonzo Church</a>'s <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lambda_calculus" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Lambda calculus">lambda calculus</a>. It quickly became the favored programming language for <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Artificial_intelligence" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Artificial intelligence">artificial intelligence</a> (AI) research. As one of the earliest programming languages, Lisp pioneered many ideas in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Computer_science" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Computer science">computer science</a>, including <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tree_data_structure" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Tree data structure">tree data structures</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Garbage_collection_(computer_science)" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Garbage collection (computer science)">automatic storage management</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dynamic_typing" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Dynamic typing">dynamic typing</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Conditional_(computer_programming)" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Conditional (computer programming)">conditionals</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Higher-order_function" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Higher-order function">higher-order functions</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Recursion_(computer_science)" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Recursion (computer science)">recursion</a>, and the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Self-hosting" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Self-hosting">self-hosting</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Compiler" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Compiler">compiler</a>.<sup style="unicode-bidi: isolate; white-space: nowrap; font-size: 11.2px; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal;"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lisp_(programming_language)#cite_note-Graham-6" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none; white-space: nowrap;">[6]</a></sup></p></div><div><br/></div><div><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; color: rgb(37, 37, 37); font-family: sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div><span style="font-size: 24px;"><b>Haskell</b></span></div><div><span style="white-space: nowrap;"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:IPA_for_English" style="text-decoration: none !important; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Help:IPA for English">/<span style="border-bottom: 1px dotted;"><span title="/ˈ/ primary stress follows">ˈ</span><span title="'h' in 'hi'">h</span><span title="/æ/ short 'a' in 'bad'">æ</span><span title="'s' in 'sigh'">s</span><span title="'k' in 'kind'">k</span><span title="/əl/ 'le' in 'bottle'">əl</span></span>/</a></span><sup style="unicode-bidi: isolate; white-space: nowrap; font-size: 11.2px; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal;"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Haskell_(programming_language)#cite_note-26" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none; white-space: nowrap;">[26]</a></sup> is a standardized, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/General-purpose_programming_language" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="General-purpose programming language">general-purpose</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Purely_functional_programming" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Purely functional programming">purely functional programming</a> language, with <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Non-strict_semantics" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Non-strict semantics">non-strict semantics</a> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Strong_typing" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Strong typing">strong</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Static_typing" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Static typing">static typing</a>.<sup style="unicode-bidi: isolate; white-space: nowrap; font-size: 11.2px; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal;"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Haskell_(programming_language)#cite_note-FOOTNOTEPeyton_Jones2003-27" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none; white-space: nowrap;">[27]</a></sup> It is named after <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Logician" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Logician">logician</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Haskell_Curry" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Haskell Curry">Haskell Curry</a>.<sup style="unicode-bidi: isolate; white-space: nowrap; font-size: 11.2px; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal;"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Haskell_(programming_language)#cite_note-FOOTNOTEHudakHughesPeyton_JonesWadler2007-1" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none; white-space: nowrap;">[1]</a></sup> The latest standard of Haskell is Haskell 2010. As of May 2016, a group is working on the next version, Haskell 2020.<sup style="unicode-bidi: isolate; white-space: nowrap; font-size: 11.2px; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal;"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Haskell_(programming_language)#cite_note-28" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none; white-space: nowrap;">[28]</a></sup></div></div><p style="margin: 0.5em 0px; color: rgb(37, 37, 37); font-family: sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">Haskell features a <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Type_system" style="text-decoration: underline; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Type system">type system</a> with <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Type_inference" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Type inference">type inference</a><sup style="unicode-bidi: isolate; white-space: nowrap; font-size: 11.2px; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal;"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Haskell_(programming_language)#cite_note-29" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none; white-space: nowrap;">[29]</a></sup> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lazy_evaluation" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Lazy evaluation">lazy evaluation</a>.<sup style="unicode-bidi: isolate; white-space: nowrap; font-size: 11.2px; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal;"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Haskell_(programming_language)#cite_note-30" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none; white-space: nowrap;">[30]</a></sup> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Type_classes" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Type classes">Type classes</a> first appeared in the Haskell programming language.<sup style="unicode-bidi: isolate; white-space: nowrap; font-size: 11.2px; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal;"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Haskell_(programming_language)#cite_note-31" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none; white-space: nowrap;">[31]</a></sup> Its main implementation is the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Glasgow_Haskell_Compiler" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Glasgow Haskell Compiler">Glasgow Haskell Compiler</a>.</p><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"><span style="font-family: sans-serif;">Haskell is based on the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Semantics_of_programming_languages" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Semantics of programming languages">semantics</a>, but not the syntax, of the language <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Miranda_(programming_language)" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Miranda (programming language)">Miranda</a>, which served to focus the efforts of the initial Haskell working group.<sup style="unicode-bidi: isolate; white-space: nowrap; font-size: 11.2px; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal;"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Haskell_(programming_language)#cite_note-32" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none; white-space: nowrap;">[32]</a></sup> Haskell is used widely in academia<sup style="unicode-bidi: isolate; white-space: nowrap; font-size: 11.2px; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal;"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Haskell_(programming_language)#cite_note-33" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none; white-space: nowrap;">[33]</a></sup><sup style="unicode-bidi: isolate; white-space: nowrap; font-size: 11.2px; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal;"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Haskell_(programming_language)#cite_note-34" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none; white-space: nowrap;">[34]</a></sup> and also used in industry.<sup style="unicode-bidi: isolate; white-space: nowrap; font-size: 11.2px; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal;"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Haskell_(programming_language)#cite_note-35" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none; white-space: nowrap;">[35]</a></sup></span></span></div><div><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"><span style="font-family: sans-serif;"><sup><span style="font-size: 11.2px;"><br/></span></sup></span></span></div><div><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; color: rgb(37, 37, 37); font-family: sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div><span style="font-size: 24px;"><b>Prolog</b></span> </div><div>is a general-purpose <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Logic_programming" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Logic programming">logic programming</a> language associated with <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Artificial_intelligence" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Artificial intelligence">artificial intelligence</a> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Computational_linguistics" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Computational linguistics">computational linguistics</a>.<sup style="unicode-bidi: isolate; white-space: nowrap; font-size: 11.2px; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal;"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Prolog#cite_note-Clocksin2003-1" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none; white-space: nowrap;">[1]</a></sup><sup style="unicode-bidi: isolate; white-space: nowrap; font-size: 11.2px; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal;"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Prolog#cite_note-Bratko2001-2" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none; white-space: nowrap;">[2]</a></sup><sup style="unicode-bidi: isolate; white-space: nowrap; font-size: 11.2px; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal;"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Prolog#cite_note-Covington1994-3" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none; white-space: nowrap;">[3]</a></sup></div></div><p style="margin: 0.5em 0px; color: rgb(37, 37, 37); font-family: sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">Prolog has its roots in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/First-order_logic" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="First-order logic">first-order logic</a>, a <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Formal_logic" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Formal logic">formal logic</a>, and unlike many other <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Programming language">programming languages</a>, Prolog is <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Declarative_programming" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Declarative programming">declarative</a>: the program logic is expressed in terms of relations, represented as facts and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Rule_of_inference" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Rule of inference">rules</a>. A computation is initiated by running a <i>query</i> over these relations.<sup style="unicode-bidi: isolate; white-space: nowrap; font-size: 11.2px; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal;"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Prolog#cite_note-lloyd84-4" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none; white-space: nowrap;">[4]</a></sup></p><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div><span style="font-family: sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);">The language was first conceived by a group around </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Alain_Colmerauer" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Alain Colmerauer">Alain Colmerauer</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"> in </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marseille" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Marseille">Marseille</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);">, </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/France" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="France">France</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);">, in the early 1970s and the first Prolog system was developed in 1972 by Colmerauer with Philippe Roussel.<sup style="unicode-bidi: isolate; white-space: nowrap; font-size: 11.2px; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal;"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Prolog#cite_note-Kowalski-5" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none; white-space: nowrap;">[5]</a></sup><sup style="unicode-bidi: isolate; white-space: nowrap; font-size: 11.2px; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal;"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Prolog#cite_note-6" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none; white-space: nowrap;">[6]</a></sup></span></span></div><div><span style="font-family: sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 11.2px;"><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"><sup><br/></sup></span></span></span></div><div><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; color: rgb(37, 37, 37); font-family: sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div><span style="font-size: 24px;"><b>Scala</b></span> </div><div>(<span style="white-space: nowrap;"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:IPA_for_English" style="text-decoration: none !important; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Help:IPA for English">/<span style="border-bottom: 1px dotted;"><span title="/ˈ/ primary stress follows">ˈ</span><span title="'s' in 'sigh'">s</span><span title="'k' in 'kind'">k</span><span title="/ɑː/ 'a' in 'father'">ɑː</span><span title="'l' in 'lie'">l</span><span title="/ɑː/ 'a' in 'father'">ɑː</span></span>/</a></span> <span title="English pronunciation respelling"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Pronunciation_respelling_key" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Help:Pronunciation respelling key"><i><b><span style="font-variant: small-caps; text-transform: lowercase;">skah</span></b>-lah</i></a></span>)<sup style="unicode-bidi: isolate; white-space: nowrap; font-size: 11.2px; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal;"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scala_(programming_language)#cite_note-9" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none; white-space: nowrap;">[9]</a></sup> is a <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/General-purpose_programming_language" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="General-purpose programming language">general-purpose</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Programming language">programming language</a>. Scala has full support for <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Functional_programming" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Functional programming">functional programming</a> and a strong <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Static_typing" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Static typing">static</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Type_system" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Type system">type system</a>. Designed to be concise,<sup style="unicode-bidi: isolate; white-space: nowrap; font-size: 11.2px; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal;"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scala_(programming_language)#cite_note-10" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none; white-space: nowrap;">[10]</a></sup> many of Scala's design decisions were inspired by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Criticism_of_Java" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Criticism of Java">criticism of Java</a>'s shortcomings.<sup style="unicode-bidi: isolate; white-space: nowrap; font-size: 11.2px; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal;"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scala_(programming_language)#cite_note-overview-8" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none; white-space: nowrap;">[8]</a></sup></div></div><p style="margin: 0.5em 0px; color: rgb(37, 37, 37); font-family: sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">Scala source code is intended to be compiled to <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Java_bytecode" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Java bytecode">Java bytecode</a>, so that the resulting executable code runs on a <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Java_virtual_machine" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Java virtual machine">Java virtual machine</a>. Java libraries may be used directly in Scala code and vice versa (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Language_interoperability" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Language interoperability">language interoperability</a>).<sup style="unicode-bidi: isolate; white-space: nowrap; font-size: 11.2px; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal;"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scala_(programming_language)#cite_note-11" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none; white-space: nowrap;">[11]</a></sup> Like Java, Scala is <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Object-oriented_programming" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Object-oriented programming">object-oriented</a>, and uses a curly-brace syntax reminiscent of the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/C_(programming_language)" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="C (programming language)">C programming language</a>. Unlike Java, Scala has many features of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Functional_programming" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Functional programming">functional programming</a> languages like <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scheme_(programming_language)" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Scheme (programming language)">Scheme</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Standard_ML" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Standard ML">Standard ML</a> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Haskell_(programming_language)" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Haskell (programming language)">Haskell</a>, including <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Currying" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Currying">currying</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Type_inference" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Type inference">type inference</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Immutability" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Immutability">immutability</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lazy_evaluation" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Lazy evaluation">lazy evaluation</a>, and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pattern_matching" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Pattern matching">pattern matching</a>. It also has an advanced type system supporting <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Algebraic_data_type" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Algebraic data type">algebraic data types</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Covariance_and_contravariance_(computer_science)" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Covariance and contravariance (computer science)">covariance and contravariance</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Higher-order_type_operator" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Higher-order type operator">higher-order types</a> (but not <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Parametric_polymorphism" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Parametric polymorphism">higher-rank types</a>), and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anonymous_type" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Anonymous type">anonymous types</a>. Other features of Scala not present in Java include <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Operator_overloading" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Operator overloading">operator overloading</a>, optional parameters, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Named_parameter" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Named parameter">named parameters</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Raw_string" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Raw string">raw strings</a>, and no <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Checked_exception" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Checked exception">checked exceptions</a>.</p><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; color: rgb(37, 37, 37); font-family: sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div>The name Scala is a <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Portmanteau" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Portmanteau">portmanteau</a> of <i>scalable</i> and <i>language</i>, signifying that it is designed to grow with the demands of its users.<sup style="unicode-bidi: isolate; white-space: nowrap; font-size: 11.2px; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal;"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scala_(programming_language)#cite_note-StepsInScala-12" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none; white-space: nowrap;">[12]</a></sup></div></div></div><div><span style="font-size: 11.2px;"><span style="font-family: sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"><sup><br/></sup></span></span></span></div><div><p style="margin: 0.5em 0px; color: rgb(37, 37, 37); font-family: sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><span style="font-size: 24px;"><b>Lua</b></span> (<span style="white-space: nowrap;"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:IPA_for_English" style="text-decoration: none !important; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Help:IPA for English">/<span style="border-bottom: 1px dotted;"><span title="/ˈ/ primary stress follows">ˈ</span><span title="'l' in 'lie'">l</span><span title="/uː/ long 'oo' in 'food'">uː</span><span title="/ə/ 'a' in 'about'">ə</span></span>/</a></span> <span title="English pronunciation respelling"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Pronunciation_respelling_key" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Help:Pronunciation respelling key"><i><b><span style="font-variant: small-caps; text-transform: lowercase;">loo</span></b>-ə</i></a></span>, from <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Portuguese_language" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Portuguese language">Portuguese</a>: <span lang="pt"><i><a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/lua#Portuguese" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(102, 51, 102); background: none;" title="wikt:lua">lua</a></i></span> <span title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:IPA_for_Portuguese" style="text-decoration: none !important; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Help:IPA for Portuguese">[ˈlu.(w)ɐ]</a></span> meaning <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Moon" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Moon">moon</a></i>) is a lightweight <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Multi-paradigm_programming_language" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Multi-paradigm programming language">multi-paradigm</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language" style="text-decoration: none;
