color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Programming language">programming language</a> designed primarily for <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Embedded_systems" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Embedded systems">embedded systems</a> and clients.<sup style="unicode-bidi: isolate; white-space: nowrap; font-size: 11.2px; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal;"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lua_(programming_language)#cite_note-luaspe-1" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none; white-space: nowrap;">[1]</a></sup> Lua is <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cross-platform" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Cross-platform">cross-platform</a> since it is written in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ANSI_C" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="ANSI C">ANSI C</a>,<sup style="unicode-bidi: isolate; white-space: nowrap; font-size: 11.2px; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal;"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lua_(programming_language)#cite_note-luaabout-2" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none; white-space: nowrap;">[2]</a></sup> and has a relatively simple <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/C_(programming_language)" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="C (programming language)">C</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Application_programming_interface" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Application programming interface">API</a>.<sup style="unicode-bidi: isolate; white-space: nowrap; font-size: 11.2px; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal;"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lua_(programming_language)#cite_note-3" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none; white-space: nowrap;">[3]</a></sup></p><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; color: rgb(37, 37, 37); font-family: sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div>Lua was originally designed in 1993 as a language for extending <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Application_software" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Application software">software applications</a> to meet the increasing demand for customization at the time. It provided the basic facilities of most <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Procedural_programming" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Procedural programming">procedural</a> programming languages, but more complicated or <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Domain-specific_language" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Domain-specific language">domain-specific</a> features were not included; rather, it included mechanisms for extending the language, allowing programmers to implement such features. As Lua was intended to be a general embeddable extension language, the designers of Lua focused on improving its speed, portability, extensibility, and ease-of-use in development.</div></div><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; color: rgb(37, 37, 37); font-family: sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"></div></div><div><br/></div><div><span style="font-size: 11.2px;"><span style="font-family: sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"><sup><br/></sup></span></span></span></div></div></div></div></div><div><hr/></div><div style="font-family: gotham, helvetica, arial, sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 18px;"><b>Programming Throwdown Summaries</b></span></div><div><div style="padding: 0.25em 0px; margin: 0px 0px 0.25em; text-indent: 0px; border: none;"><div><span style="color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><span style="font-family: Arial, Tahoma, Helvetica, FreeSans, sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 22px;"><b><br/></b></span></span></span></div></div></div><div><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div></div><div><span style="font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"><br/></span></span></span></div><div><hr/></div><div><span style="font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);">The <b>V8 JavaScript Engine</b> is an </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Open_source" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Open source">open source</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"> </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/JavaScript_engine" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="JavaScript engine">JavaScript engine</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"> developed by The Chromium Project for the </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Google_Chrome" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Google Chrome">Google Chrome</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"> web browser.<sup style="unicode-bidi: isolate; white-space: nowrap; font-size: 11.2px; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal;"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/V8_(JavaScript_engine)#cite_note-comic-5" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none; white-space: nowrap;">[5]</a></sup> It has seen use in many other projects, such as </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Couchbase" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Couchbase">Couchbase</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);">, </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/MongoDB" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="MongoDB">MongoDB</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"> and </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Node.js" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Node.js">Node.js</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);">that are used server side. As of 2012, the head programmer is </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lars_Bak_(computer_programmer)" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Lars Bak (computer programmer)">Lars Bak</a></span><span style="font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Arial, sans;"><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"><span style="font-family: sans-serif;">.<sup style="unicode-bidi: isolate; white-space: nowrap; font-size: 11.2px; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal;"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/V8_(JavaScript_engine)#cite_note-6" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none; white-space: nowrap;">[6]</a></sup> The first version of the V8 engine was released at the same time as the first version of Chrome, September 2, 2008.</span></span></span></span></div></div></div><div><div style="font-family:&quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Arial, sans;font-size:16px;"><br/></div><hr style="font-family:&quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Arial, sans;font-size:16px;"/><div style="font-family:&quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Arial, sans;font-size:16px;"><span style="color: rgb(108, 108, 108); font-family: &quot;NeueHaasGroteskText W01&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); display: inline !important; float: none;"><b>MIS (management information systems) i</b></span><span style="color: rgb(108, 108, 108); font-family: &quot;NeueHaasGroteskText W01&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); display: inline !important; float: none;">s the department controlling hardware and software systems used for business-critical decision-making within an </span><a href="http://searchwindowsserver.techtarget.com/definition/enterprise" style="text-decoration: underline; color: rgb(0, 179, 172); transition: color 0.2s; font-family: &quot;NeueHaasGroteskText W01&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">enterprise</a><span style="color: rgb(108, 108, 108); font-family: &quot;NeueHaasGroteskText W01&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); display: inline !important; float: none;">.</span></div><div style="font-family:&quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Arial, sans;font-size:16px;"><b><span style="font-size: 24px;"><br/></span></b></div><div style="font-family:&quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Arial, sans;font-size:16px;"><span style="font-size: 24px;"><b>Bitmasks</b></span></div></div><div><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);font-family:gotham, helvetica, arial, sans-serif;font-size:14px;"><div style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px 0px 10px; padding-bottom: 10px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247);"><div style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px 0px 10px; padding-bottom: 10px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247);"><div style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px 0px 10px; padding-bottom: 10px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247);"><div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px 0px 10px; padding-bottom: 10px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247);"><div style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px 0px 10px; padding-bottom: 10px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247);"><div style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px 0px 10px; padding-bottom: 10px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247);"><div style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px 0px 10px; padding-bottom: 10px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247);"><div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px 0px 10px; padding-bottom: 10px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247);"><div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px 0px 10px; padding-bottom: 10px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247);"><div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px 0px 10px; padding-bottom: 10px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247);"><div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px 0px 10px; padding-bottom: 10px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247);"><div><div style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-size: 15px; clear: both; font-family: Arial, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div><span style="color: rgb(36, 39, 41);">By performing binary operations on the mask and the state one could achieve the following:</span></div><div><span style="color: rgb(36, 39, 41);"><br/></span></div><div><span style="color: rgb(36, 39, 41);"><span style="font-family: Arial, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, sans-serif;">The AND operator extracts a subset of the bits in the state</span></span></div><ul><li><span style="font-family: Arial, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(36, 39, 41);">The OR operator sets a subset of the bits in the state</span></span></li><li><span style="font-family: Arial, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(36, 39, 41);">The XOR operator toggles a subset of the bits in the state</span></span></li></ul></div><div style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-size: 15px; clear: both; color: rgb(36, 39, 41); font-family: Arial, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div>If we want to set a particular value to true, we could do this by using the OR operator and the following bit mask:</div></div><pre style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 5px; border: 0px; font-size: 13px; width: auto; max-height: 600px; overflow: auto; font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, &quot;Lucida Console&quot;, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, &quot;DejaVu Sans Mono&quot;, &quot;Bitstream Vera Sans Mono&quot;, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace, sans-serif; background-color: rgb(239, 240, 241); word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(36, 39, 41); font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;"><code style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-size: 13px; font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, &quot;Lucida Console&quot;, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, &quot;DejaVu Sans Mono&quot;, &quot;Bitstream Vera Sans Mono&quot;, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace, sans-serif; background-color: rgb(239, 240, 241); white-space: inherit;">Mask:   10000000b
Value:  00000101b
---- OR ---------
Result: 10000101b
</code></pre><p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-size: 15px; clear: both; color: rgb(36, 39, 41); font-family: Arial, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">Or one could select a particular value from the state by using the AND operator:</p><pre style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 5px; border: 0px; font-size: 13px; width: auto; max-height: 600px; overflow: auto; font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, &quot;Lucida Console&quot;, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, &quot;DejaVu Sans Mono&quot;, &quot;Bitstream Vera Sans Mono&quot;, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace, sans-serif; background-color: rgb(239, 240, 241); word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(36, 39, 41); font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;"><code style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-size: 13px; font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, &quot;Lucida Console&quot;, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, &quot;DejaVu Sans Mono&quot;, &quot;Bitstream Vera Sans Mono&quot;, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace, sans-serif; background-color: rgb(239, 240, 241); white-space: inherit;">Mask:   00000100b
Value:  00000101b
---- AND ---------
Result: 00000100b
</code></pre><div style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-size: 15px; clear: both; color: rgb(36, 39, 41); font-family: Arial, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div>I suggest you to take some deeper look into it and get familiar with the jargon. A good start may be <a href="http://codeforces.com/blog/entry/18169" rel="nofollow" style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-size: 15px; color: rgb(0, 89, 153); text-decoration: none; cursor: pointer;">this</a> link.</div></div></div><hr/><div><b><span style="font-size: 19px;">S.O.L.I.D STANDS FOR:</span></b></div><div>When expanded the acronyms might seem complicated, but they are pretty simple to grasp.</div><div><br/></div><div><b>S – Single-responsiblity principle</b></div><div>A class should have one and only one reason to change, meaning that a class should have only one job.</div><div>Read: Linux commands do one job really well, then they are piped. Or, think Gulp.</div><div><br/></div><div><b>O – Open-closed principle</b></div><div>Objects or entities should be open for extension, but closed for modification.</div><div>Think NPM... don't touch the packages... make calls to them... extend them.</div><div><br/></div><div><b>- L – Liskov substitution principle</b></div><div>&quot;Let q(x) be a property provable about objects of x of type T. Then q(y) should be provable for objects y of type S where S is a subtype of T.&quot;</div><div><i>All this is stating is that every subclass/derived class should be substitutable for their base/parent class.</i></div><div><br/></div><div><b>- I – Interface segregation principle</b></div><div>A client should never be forced to implement an interface that it doesn’t use or clients shouldn’t be forced to depend on methods they do not use.</div><div>Think MVC -- Very basic shit.</div><div><br/></div><div><b>- D – Dependency Inversion Principle</b></div><div>Entities must depend on abstractions not on concretions. It states that the high level module must not depend on the low level module, but they should depend on abstractions.</div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px 0px 10px; padding-bottom: 10px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247);"><div><span style="font-size: 23px;"><span style="font-family: Lora, Georgia, serif;"><span style="color: rgb(85, 85, 85);"><br/></span></span></span></div><hr/><div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px 0px 10px; font-family: Lora, Georgia, serif; font-size: 15px; padding-bottom: 10px; color: rgb(85, 85, 85); font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247);"><div><span style="font-size: 21px;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box; font-weight: bold; font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, Helvetica, sans-serif;">Counting sort</strong></span></div><div>is a very time-efficient (and somewhat space-inefficient) algorithm for sorting that avoids comparisons and exploits the <span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-size: 11.805px;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 400; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 1.21em; font-family: KaTeX_Main; white-space: nowrap;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; clip: rect(1px 1px 1px 1px); overflow: hidden; position: absolute !important; padding: 0px !important; border: 0px !important; height: 1px !important; width: 1px !important;">O(1)</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; display: inline-block;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; display: inline-block;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: KaTeX_Math; font-style: italic; margin-right: 0.02778em;">O</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">(</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">1</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span> time insertions and lookups in <span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">a list</span></span>.</div></div><p style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px 0px 10px; font-family: Lora, Georgia, serif; font-size: 15px; padding-bottom: 10px; color: rgb(85, 85, 85); font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); text-decoration-style: initial; text-decoration-color: initial;">The idea is simple: if you're sorting  integers and you know they all fall in the range <span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-size: 11.805px;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 400; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 1.21em; font-family: KaTeX_Main; white-space: nowrap;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; clip: rect(1px 1px 1px 1px); overflow: hidden; position: absolute !important; padding: 0px !important; border: 0px !important; height: 1px !important; width: 1px !important;">1..100</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; display: inline-block;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; display: inline-block;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">1</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">.</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">.</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">1</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">0</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">0</span></span></span></span></span>, you can generate a sorted <span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">list</span></span> this way:</p><ul style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 10px; padding-bottom: 10px; color: rgb(85, 85, 85); font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 15px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); text-decoration-style: initial; text-decoration-color: initial;"><li style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Lora, Georgia, serif; font-size: 15px;">Allocate <span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">a list</span></span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Inconsolata, &quot;Droid Mono&quot;, &quot;Courier New&quot;;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">num_counts</span></span> where the indices represent numbers from our input <span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">list</span></span> and the values represent how many times the index number appears. Start each value at 0.</li><li style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Lora, Georgia, serif; font-size: 15px;">In one pass of the input <span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">list</span></span>, update <span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Inconsolata, &quot;Droid Mono&quot;, &quot;Courier New&quot;;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">num_counts</span></span> as you go, so that at the end the values in <span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Inconsolata, &quot;Droid Mono&quot;, &quot;Courier New&quot;;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">num_counts</span></span> are correct.</li><li style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Lora, Georgia, serif; font-size: 15px;">Allocate <span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">a list</span></span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Inconsolata, &quot;Droid Mono&quot;, &quot;Courier New&quot;;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">sorted_list</span></span> where we'll store our sorted numbers.</li><li style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Lora, Georgia, serif; font-size: 15px;">In one in-order pass of <span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Inconsolata, &quot;Droid Mono&quot;, &quot;Courier New&quot;;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">num_counts</span></span> put each number, the correct number of times, into <span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Inconsolata, &quot;Droid Mono&quot;, &quot;Courier New&quot;;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">sorted_list</span></span>.</li></ul></div><hr/><div><span style="color: rgb(85, 85, 85);"><span style="font-size: 15px;"><span style="font-family: Lora, Georgia, serif;"><span style="font-size: 23px;">A problem has <strong style="box-sizing: border-box; font-weight: bold; font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, Helvetica, sans-serif;">overlapping subproblems</strong></span></span></span></span></div><div><span style="color: rgb(85, 85, 85);"><span style="font-size: 15px;"><span style="font-family: Lora, Georgia, serif;">if finding its solution involves solving the <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">same</em>subproblem multiple times.</span></span></span></div><div><span style="color: rgb(85, 85, 85);"><span style="font-size: 15px;"><span style="font-family: Lora, Georgia, serif;">As an example, let's look at the fibonacci squence (the series where each number is the sum of the two previous ones—0,1,1,2,3,5,8...).</span></span></span></div><div></div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247);"><div style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px 0px 10px; padding-bottom: 10px;"><div><span style="color: rgb(85, 85, 85);"><span style="font-size: 15px;"><span style="font-family: Lora, Georgia, serif;">Our function ends up recursively calling </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Inconsolata, &quot;Droid Mono&quot;, &quot;Courier New&quot;;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">fib(2)</span></span><span style="font-family: Lora, Georgia, serif;"> </span><strong style="box-sizing: border-box; font-weight: bold; font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, Helvetica, sans-serif;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">three times</em></strong></span><span style="font-family: Lora, Georgia, serif;"><span style="font-size: 15px;">. So the problem of finding the </span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-size: 11.805px;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 400; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 1.21em; font-family: KaTeX_Main; white-space: nowrap;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; clip: rect(1px 1px 1px 1px); overflow: hidden; position: absolute !important; padding: 0px !important; border: 0px !important; height: 1px !important; width: 1px !important;">n</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; display: inline-block;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; display: inline-block;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: KaTeX_Math; font-style: italic;">n</span></span></span></span></span><span style="font-size: 15px;">th fibonacci number has overlapping subproblems.</span></span></span></div></div></div></div><hr/><div style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px 0px 10px; font-family: Lora, Georgia, serif; font-size: 15px; padding-bottom: 10px; color: rgb(85, 85, 85); font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247);"><div><span style="font-size: 23px;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box; font-weight: bold; font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, Helvetica, sans-serif;">Memoization</strong></span></div><div>ensures that a function doesn't run for the same inputs more than once by keeping a record of the results for given inputs (usually in <span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">a dictionary</span></span>).</div></div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px 0px 10px; padding-bottom: 10px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247);"><div><span style="font-size: 15px;"><span style="font-family: Lora, Georgia, serif;"><span style="color: rgb(85, 85, 85);">For example, a simple recursive function for computing the <span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-size: 11.805px;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 400; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 1.21em; font-family: KaTeX_Main; white-space: nowrap;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; clip: rect(1px 1px 1px 1px); overflow: hidden; position: absolute !important; padding: 0px !important; border: 0px !important; height: 1px !important; width: 1px !important;">n</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; display: inline-block;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; display: inline-block;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: KaTeX_Math; font-style: italic;">n</span></span></span></span></span>th fibonacci number:</span></span></span></div><div></div></div><hr/><div style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px 0px 10px; font-family: Lora, Georgia, serif; font-size: 15px; padding-bottom: 10px; color: rgb(85, 85, 85); font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247);"><div><span style="font-size: 21px;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box; font-weight: bold; font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, Helvetica, sans-serif;">Big O notation</strong></span></div><div><strong style="box-sizing: border-box; font-weight: bold; font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, Helvetica, sans-serif;">is the language we use for articulating how long an algorithm takes to run</strong>. It's how we compare the efficiency of different approaches to a problem.</div></div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px 0px 10px; padding-bottom: 10px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247);"><div><span style="font-size: 15px;"><span style="font-family: Lora, Georgia, serif;"><span style="color: rgb(85, 85, 85);">With big O notation we express the runtime in terms of—brace yourself—<span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><i>how quickly it grows relative to the input, as the input gets arbitrarily large</i>. </span></span></span></span> <strong style="box-sizing: border-box; font-weight: bold; font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, Helvetica, sans-serif; color: rgb(85, 85, 85); font-size: 15px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); text-decoration-style: initial; text-decoration-color: initial;">how quickly the runtime grows</strong><span style="color: rgb(85, 85, 85); font-family: Lora, Georgia, serif; font-size: 15px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); text-decoration-style: initial; text-decoration-color: initial; display: inline !important; float: none;">—, </span> <strong style="box-sizing: border-box; font-weight: bold; font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, Helvetica, sans-serif; color: rgb(85, 85, 85); font-size: 15px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); text-decoration-style: initial; text-decoration-color: initial;">relative to the input</strong><span style="color: rgb(85, 85, 85); font-family: Lora, Georgia, serif; font-size: 15px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); text-decoration-style: initial; text-decoration-color: initial; display: inline !important; float: none;">—, </span> <strong style="box-sizing: border-box; font-weight: bold; font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, Helvetica, sans-serif; color: rgb(85, 85, 85); font-size: 15px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); text-decoration-style: initial; text-decoration-color: initial;">as the input gets arbitrarily large</strong><span style="color: rgb(85, 85, 85); font-family: Lora, Georgia, serif; font-size: 15px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); text-decoration-style: initial; text-decoration-color: initial; display: inline !important; float: none;">—</span></div><div><br/></div><div>Big O notation is like math except it's an awesome, not-boring kind of math where you get to wave your hands through the details and just focus on what's basically happening.</div><div><br/></div></div><hr/><div><span style="color: rgb(85, 85, 85);"><span style="font-size: 15px;"><span style="font-family: Lora, Georgia, serif;"><span style="font-size: 20px;">Going <strong style="box-sizing: border-box; font-weight: bold; font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, Helvetica, sans-serif;">bottom-up</strong></span></span></span></span></div><div><span style="color: rgb(85, 85, 85);"><span style="font-size: 15px;"><span style="font-family: Lora, Georgia, serif;">is a way to avoid recursion, saving the </span><strong style="box-sizing: border-box; font-weight: bold; font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, Helvetica, sans-serif;">memory cost</strong><span style="font-family: Lora, Georgia, serif;"> that recursion incurs when it builds up the </span><strong style="box-sizing: border-box; font-weight: bold; font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, Helvetica, sans-serif;">call stack</strong><span style="font-family: Lora, Georgia, serif;">.</span></span></span></div></div><p style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px 0px 10px; font-family: Lora, Georgia, serif; font-size: 15px; padding-bottom: 10px; color: rgb(85, 85, 85); font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); text-decoration-style: initial; text-decoration-color: initial;">Put simply, a bottom-up algorithm &quot;starts from the beginning,&quot; while a recursive algorithm often &quot;starts from the end and works backwards.&quot;</p><p style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px 0px 10px; font-family: Lora, Georgia, serif; font-size: 15px; padding-bottom: 10px; color: rgb(85, 85, 85); font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); text-decoration-style: initial; text-decoration-color: initial;">For example, if we wanted to multiply all the numbers in the range <span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-size: 11.805px;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 400; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 1.21em; font-family: KaTeX_Main; white-space: nowrap;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; clip: rect(1px 1px 1px 1px); overflow: hidden; position: absolute !important; padding: 0px !important; border: 0px !important; height: 1px !important; width: 1px !important;">1...n</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; display: inline-block;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; display: inline-block;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">1</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">.</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">.</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">.</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: KaTeX_Math; font-style: italic;">n</span></span></span></span></span>, we could use this cute, <strong style="box-sizing: border-box; font-weight: bold; font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, Helvetica, sans-serif;">top-down</strong>, recursive one-liner:</p><div style="box-sizing: border-box; padding-bottom: 0px; margin-bottom: 18px; display: block; width: 680px; position: relative; background: rgb(251, 251, 251); color: rgb(85, 85, 85); font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 15px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; text-decoration-style: initial; text-decoration-color: initial;"><pre style="box-sizing: border-box; overflow: auto; font-family: Consolas, Monaco, &quot;Andale Mono&quot;, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, monospace; font-size: 0px; display: block; padding: 10px 18px; margin: 0.5em 0px; color: rgb(105, 104, 103); word-break: normal; word-wrap: break-word; background: transparent; border-width: 1px 1px 1px 5px; border-style: solid; border-color: rgb(91, 192, 222); border-image: initial; border-radius: 4px; white-space: pre; text-shadow: white 0px 1px; direction: ltr; text-align: left; word-spacing: normal; tab-size: 4; hyphens: none; width: 680px;">  <code style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, Monaco, &quot;Andale Mono&quot;, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, monospace; font-size: 12px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(105, 104, 103); background-color: transparent; border-radius: 0px; white-space: pre; text-shadow: white 0px 1px; direction: ltr; text-align: left; word-spacing: normal; word-break: normal; tab-size: 4; hyphens: none; width: auto; display: inline-block; margin-top: 3px; font-weight: 300;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(0, 91, 154);">def</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(0, 91, 154);">product_1_to_n</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(153, 153, 153);">(</span>n<span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(153, 153, 153);">)</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(153, 153, 153);">:</span>
    <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(181, 181, 181);"># we assume n &gt;= 1</span>
    <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(0, 91, 154);">return</span> n <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(0, 91, 154); background: none;">*</span> product_1_to_n<span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(153, 153, 153);">(</span>n<span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(1, 145, 200);">-1</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(153, 153, 153);">)</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(0, 91, 154);">if</span> n <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(0, 91, 154); background: none;">&gt;</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(1, 145, 200);">1</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(0, 91, 154);">else</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(1, 145, 200);">1</span></code></pre></div><p style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px 0px 10px; font-family: Lora, Georgia, serif; font-size: 15px; padding-bottom: 10px; color: rgb(85, 85, 85); font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); text-decoration-style: initial; text-decoration-color: initial;">This approach has a problem: it builds up a <strong style="box-sizing: border-box; font-weight: bold; font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, Helvetica, sans-serif;">call stack</strong> of size <span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-size: 11.805px;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 400; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 1.21em; font-family: KaTeX_Main; white-space: nowrap;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; clip: rect(1px 1px 1px 1px); overflow: hidden; position: absolute !important; padding: 0px !important; border: 0px !important; height: 1px !important; width: 1px !important;">O(n)</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; display: inline-block;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; display: inline-block;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: KaTeX_Math; font-style: italic; margin-right: 0.02778em;">O</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">(</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: KaTeX_Math; font-style: italic;">n</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span>, which makes our total memory cost <span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-size: 11.805px;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 400; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 1.21em; font-family: KaTeX_Main; white-space: nowrap;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; clip: rect(1px 1px 1px 1px); overflow: hidden; position: absolute !important; padding: 0px !important; border: 0px !important; height: 1px !important; width: 1px !important;">O(n)</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; display: inline-block;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; display: inline-block;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: KaTeX_Math; font-style: italic; margin-right: 0.02778em;">O</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">(</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: KaTeX_Math; font-style: italic;">n</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span>. This makes it vulnerable to a <strong style="box-sizing: border-box; font-weight: bold; font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, Helvetica, sans-serif;">stack overflow error</strong>, where the call stack gets too big and runs out of space.</p><p style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px 0px 10px; font-family: Lora, Georgia, serif; font-size: 15px; padding-bottom: 10px; color: rgb(85, 85, 85); font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); text-decoration-style: initial; text-decoration-color: initial;">To avoid this, we can instead go <strong style="box-sizing: border-box; font-weight: bold; font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, Helvetica, sans-serif;">bottom-up</strong>:</p><div style="box-sizing: border-box; padding-bottom: 0px; margin-bottom: 18px; display: block; width: 680px; position: relative; background: rgb(251, 251, 251); color: rgb(85, 85, 85); font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 15px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; text-decoration-style: initial; text-decoration-color: initial;"><pre style="box-sizing: border-box; overflow: auto; font-family: Consolas, Monaco, &quot;Andale Mono&quot;, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, monospace; font-size: 0px; display: block; padding: 10px 18px; margin: 0.5em 0px; color: rgb(105, 104, 103); word-break: normal; word-wrap: break-word; background: transparent; border-width: 1px 1px 1px 5px; border-style: solid; border-color: rgb(91, 192, 222); border-image: initial; border-radius: 4px; white-space: pre; text-shadow: white 0px 1px; direction: ltr; text-align: left; word-spacing: normal; tab-size: 4; hyphens: none; width: 680px;">  <code style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, Monaco, &quot;Andale Mono&quot;, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, monospace; font-size: 12px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(105, 104, 103); background-color: transparent; border-radius: 0px; white-space: pre; text-shadow: white 0px 1px; direction: ltr; text-align: left; word-spacing: normal; word-break: normal; tab-size: 4; hyphens: none; width: auto; display: inline-block; margin-top: 3px; font-weight: 300;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(0, 91, 154);">def</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(0, 91, 154);">product_1_to_n</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(153, 153, 153);">(</span>n<span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(153, 153, 153);">)</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(153, 153, 153);">:</span>
    <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(181, 181, 181);"># we assume n &gt;= 1</span>

    result <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(0, 91, 154); background: none;">=</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(1, 145, 200);">1</span>
    <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(0, 91, 154);">for</span> num <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(0, 91, 154);">in</span> range<span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(153, 153, 153);">(</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(1, 145, 200);">1</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(153, 153, 153);">,</span> n<span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(0, 91, 154); background: none;">+</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(1, 145, 200);">1</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(153, 153, 153);">)</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(153, 153, 153);">:</span>
        result <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(0, 91, 154); background: none;">*=</span> num

    <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(0, 91, 154);">return</span> result</code></pre></div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px 0px 10px; font-family: Lora, Georgia, serif; font-size: 15px; padding-bottom: 10px; color: rgb(85, 85, 85); font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247);"><div>This approach uses <span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-size: 11.805px;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 400; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 1.21em; font-family: KaTeX_Main; white-space: nowrap;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; clip: rect(1px 1px 1px 1px); overflow: hidden; position: absolute !important; padding: 0px !important; border: 0px !important; height: 1px !important; width: 1px !important;">O(1)</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; display: inline-block;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; display: inline-block;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: KaTeX_Math; font-style: italic; margin-right: 0.02778em;">O</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">(</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">1</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span> space (<span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-size: 11.805px;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 400; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 1.21em; font-family: KaTeX_Main; white-space: nowrap;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; clip: rect(1px 1px 1px 1px); overflow: hidden; position: absolute !important; padding: 0px !important; border: 0px !important; height: 1px !important; width: 1px !important;">O(n)</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; display: inline-block;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; display: inline-block;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: KaTeX_Math; font-style: italic; margin-right: 0.02778em;">O</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">(</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: KaTeX_Math; font-style: italic;">n</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span> time).</div><div><br/></div></div></div><hr/><div><span style="color: rgb(85, 85, 85);"><span style="font-size: 15px;"><span style="font-family: Lora, Georgia, serif;"><b>A closure</b></span></span></span></div><div><span style="color: rgb(85, 85, 85);"><span style="font-size: 15px;"><span style="font-family: Lora, Georgia, serif;">is a function that accesses a variable &quot;outside&quot; itself. For example:</span></span></span></div></div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; padding-bottom: 0px; margin-bottom: 18px; display: block; width: 680px; position: relative; background: rgb(251, 251, 251); color: rgb(85, 85, 85); font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 15px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; text-decoration-style: initial; text-decoration-color: initial;"><pre style="box-sizing: border-box; overflow: auto; font-family: Consolas, Monaco, &quot;Andale Mono&quot;, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, monospace; font-size: 0px; display: block; padding: 10px 18px; margin: 0.5em 0px; color: rgb(105, 104, 103); word-break: normal; word-wrap: break-word; background: transparent; border-width: 1px 1px 1px 5px; border-style: solid; border-color: rgb(91, 192, 222); border-image: initial; border-radius: 4px; white-space: pre; text-shadow: white 0px 1px; direction: ltr; text-align: left; word-spacing: normal; tab-size: 4; hyphens: none; width: 680px;">  <code style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, Monaco, &quot;Andale Mono&quot;, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, monospace; font-size: 12px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(105, 104, 103); background-color: transparent; border-radius: 0px; white-space: pre; text-shadow: white 0px 1px; direction: ltr; text-align: left; word-spacing: normal; word-break: normal; tab-size: 4; hyphens: none; width: auto; display: inline-block; margin-top: 3px; font-weight: 300;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(0, 91, 154);">var</span> message <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(0, 91, 154); background: none;">=</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(105, 174, 201);">'The British are coming.'</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(153, 153, 153);">;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(0, 91, 154);">function</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(0, 91, 154);">sayMessage</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(153, 153, 153);">(</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(153, 153, 153);">)</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(153, 153, 153);">{</span>
    <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(0, 91, 154);">alert</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(153, 153, 153);">(</span>message<span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(153, 153, 153);">)</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(153, 153, 153);">;</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(181, 181, 181);">// here we have access to message,</span>
    <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(181, 181, 181);">// even though it's declared outside this function!</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(153, 153, 153);">}</span></code></pre><span style="box-sizing: border-box; position: absolute; top: 5px; right: 7px; font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-weight: 300; color: rgb(153, 153, 153); cursor: default; font-size: 11px !important;">JavaScript</span></div><p style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px 0px 10px; font-family: Lora, Georgia, serif; font-size: 15px; padding-bottom: 10px; color: rgb(85, 85, 85); font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); text-decoration-style: initial; text-decoration-color: initial;">We'd say that <span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Inconsolata, &quot;Droid Mono&quot;, &quot;Courier New&quot;;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">message</span></span> is &quot;closed over&quot; by <span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Inconsolata, &quot;Droid Mono&quot;, &quot;Courier New&quot;;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">sayMessage</span></span>()</span>.</p><p style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px 0px 10px; font-family: Lora, Georgia, serif; font-size: 15px; padding-bottom: 10px; color: rgb(85, 85, 85); font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); text-decoration-style: initial; text-decoration-color: initial;">One useful thing to do with a closure is to create something like an &quot;instance variable&quot; that can change over time and can affect the behavior of a function.</p><div style="box-sizing: border-box; padding-bottom: 0px; margin-bottom: 18px; display: block; width: 680px; position: relative; background: rgb(251, 251, 251); color: rgb(85, 85, 85); font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 15px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; text-decoration-style: initial; text-decoration-color: initial;"><pre style="box-sizing: border-box; overflow: auto; font-family: Consolas, Monaco, &quot;Andale Mono&quot;, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, monospace; font-size: 0px; display: block; padding: 10px 18px; margin: 0.5em 0px; color: rgb(105, 104, 103); word-break: normal; word-wrap: break-word; background: transparent; border-width: 1px 1px 1px 5px; border-style: solid; border-color: rgb(91, 192, 222); border-image: initial; border-radius: 4px; white-space: pre; text-shadow: white 0px 1px; direction: ltr; text-align: left; word-spacing: normal; tab-size: 4; hyphens: none; width: 680px;">  <code style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, Monaco, &quot;Andale Mono&quot;, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, monospace; font-size: 12px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(105, 104, 103); background-color: transparent; border-radius: 0px; white-space: pre; text-shadow: white 0px 1px; direction: ltr; text-align: left; word-spacing: normal; word-break: normal; tab-size: 4; hyphens: none; width: auto; display: inline-block; margin-top: 3px; font-weight: 300;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(181, 181, 181);">// function for getting the id of a dom element,</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(181, 181, 181);">// giving it a new, unique id if it doesn't have an id yet</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(0, 91, 154);">var</span> getUniqueId <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(0, 91, 154); background: none;">=</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(153, 153, 153);">(</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(0, 91, 154);">function</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(153, 153, 153);">(</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(153, 153, 153);">)</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(153, 153, 153);">{</span>
    <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(0, 91, 154);">var</span> nextGeneratedId <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(0, 91, 154); background: none;">=</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(1, 145, 200);">0</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(153, 153, 153);">;</span>
    <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(0, 91, 154);">return</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(0, 91, 154);">function</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(153, 153, 153);">(</span>element<span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(153, 153, 153);">)</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(153, 153, 153);">{</span>
        <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(0, 91, 154);">if</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(153, 153, 153);">(</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(0, 91, 154); background: none;">!</span>element<span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(153, 153, 153);">.</span>id<span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(153, 153, 153);">)</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(153, 153, 153);">{</span>
            element<span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(153, 153, 153);">.</span>id <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(0, 91, 154); background: none;">=</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(105, 174, 201);">'generated-uid-'</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(0, 91, 154); background: none;">+</span> nextGeneratedId<span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(153, 153, 153);">;</span>
            nextGeneratedId<span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(0, 91, 154); background: none;">++</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(153, 153, 153);">;</span>
        <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(153, 153, 153);">}</span>
        <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(0, 91, 154);">return</span> element<span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(153, 153, 153);">.</span>id<span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(153, 153, 153);">;</span>
    <span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(153, 153, 153);">}</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(153, 153, 153);">;</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(153, 153, 153);">}</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(153, 153, 153);">)</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(153, 153, 153);">(</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(153, 153, 153);">)</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(153, 153, 153);">;</span></code></pre><span style="box-sizing: border-box; position: absolute; top: 5px; right: 7px; font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-weight: 300; color: rgb(153, 153, 153); cursor: default; font-size: 11px !important;">JavaScript</span></div><div style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px 0px 10px; font-family: Lora, Georgia, serif; font-size: 15px; padding-bottom: 10px; color: rgb(85, 85, 85); font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247);"><div><strong style="box-sizing: border-box; font-weight: bold; font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, Helvetica, sans-serif;">Why did we put <span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Inconsolata, &quot;Droid Mono&quot;, &quot;Courier New&quot;;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">nextGeneratedId</span></span> in an immediately-executed anonymous function?</strong> It makes <span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Inconsolata, &quot;Droid Mono&quot;, &quot;Courier New&quot;;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">nextGeneratedId</span></span> private, which prevents accidental changes from the outside world:</div></div></div><hr/><div><span style="color: rgb(85, 85, 85);"><span style="font-size: 15px;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box; font-weight: bold; font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, Helvetica, sans-serif;">Array slicing</strong></span></span></div><div><span style="color: rgb(85, 85, 85);"><span style="font-size: 15px;"><span style="font-family: Lora, Georgia, serif;">involves taking a subset from an array and </span><strong style="box-sizing: border-box; font-weight: bold; font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, Helvetica, sans-serif;">allocating a new array with those elements</strong><span style="font-family: Lora, Georgia, serif;">.</span></span></span></div></div><p style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px 0px 10px; font-family: Lora, Georgia, serif; font-size: 15px; padding-bottom: 10px;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(85, 85, 85); font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 15px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); text-decoration-style: initial; text-decoration-color: initial;">In <span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">Python</span></span> you can create a new <span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">list</span></span> of the elements in <span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Inconsolata, &quot;Droid Mono&quot;, &quot;Courier New&quot;;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">my_list</span></span>, from <span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Inconsolata, &quot;Droid Mono&quot;, &quot;Courier New&quot;;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">start_index</span></span> to <span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Inconsolata, &quot;Droid Mono&quot;, &quot;Courier New&quot;;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">end_index</span></span>(exclusive), like this:</span></p><div style="box-sizing: border-box; padding-bottom: 0px; margin-bottom: 18px; display: block; width: 680px; position: relative; background: rgb(251, 251, 251);"><pre style="box-sizing: border-box; overflow: auto; font-family: Consolas, Monaco, &quot;Andale Mono&quot;, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, monospace; font-size: 0px; display: block; padding: 10px 18px; margin: 0.5em 0px; color: rgb(105, 104, 103); word-break: normal; word-wrap: break-word; background: transparent; border-width: 1px 1px 1px 5px; border-style: solid; border-color: rgb(91, 192, 222); border-image: initial; border-radius: 4px; white-space: pre; text-shadow: white 0px 1px; direction: ltr; text-align: left; word-spacing: normal; tab-size: 4; hyphens: none; width: 680px;">  <code style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, Monaco, &quot;Andale Mono&quot;, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, monospace; font-size: 12px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(105, 104, 103); background-color: transparent; border-radius: 0px; white-space: pre; text-shadow: white 0px 1px; direction: ltr; text-align: left; word-spacing: normal; word-break: normal; tab-size: 4; hyphens: none; width: auto; display: inline-block; margin-top: 3px; font-weight: 300;">my_list<span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(153, 153, 153);">[</span>start_index<span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(153, 153, 153);">:</span>end_index<span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(153, 153, 153);">]</span></code></pre><span style="box-sizing: border-box; position: absolute; top: 5px; right: 7px; font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-weight: 300; color: rgb(153, 153, 153); cursor: default; font-size: 11px !important;">Python</span></div><p style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px 0px 10px; font-family: Lora, Georgia, serif; font-size: 15px; padding-bottom: 10px;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(85, 85, 85); font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 15px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); text-decoration-style: initial; text-decoration-color: initial;">You can also get everything <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">after</em> <span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Inconsolata, &quot;Droid Mono&quot;, &quot;Courier New&quot;;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">start_index</span></span> by just omitting <span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Inconsolata, &quot;Droid Mono&quot;, &quot;Courier New&quot;;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">end_index</span></span>:</span></p><div style="box-sizing: border-box; padding-bottom: 0px; margin-bottom: 18px; display: block; width: auto; position: relative; background: rgb(251, 251, 251);"><pre style="box-sizing: border-box; overflow: auto; font-family: Consolas, Monaco, &quot;Andale Mono&quot;, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, monospace; font-size: 0px; display: block; padding: 10px 18px; margin: 0.5em 0px; color: rgb(105, 104, 103); word-break: normal; word-wrap: break-word; background: transparent; border-width: 1px 1px 1px 5px; border-style: solid; border-color: rgb(91, 192, 222); border-image: initial; border-radius: 4px; white-space: pre; text-shadow: white 0px 1px; direction: ltr; text-align: left; word-spacing: normal; tab-size: 4; hyphens: none; width: 680px;">  <code style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, Monaco, &quot;Andale Mono&quot;, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, monospace; font-size: 12px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(105, 104, 103); background-color: transparent; border-radius: 0px; white-space: pre; text-shadow: white 0px 1px; direction: ltr; text-align: left; word-spacing: normal; word-break: normal; tab-size: 4; hyphens: none; width: auto; display: inline-block; margin-top: 3px; font-weight: 300;">my_list<span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(153, 153, 153);">[</span>start_index<span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(153, 153, 153);">:</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(153, 153, 153);">]</span></code></pre><span style="box-sizing: border-box; position: absolute; top: 5px; right: 7px; font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-weight: 300; color: rgb(153, 153, 153); cursor: default; font-size: 11px !important;">Python</span></div><p style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px 0px 10px; font-family: Lora, Georgia, serif; font-size: 15px; padding-bottom: 10px;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(85, 85, 85); font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 15px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); text-decoration-style: initial; text-decoration-color: initial;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box; font-weight: bold; font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, Helvetica, sans-serif;">Careful: there's a hidden time and space cost here!</strong> It's tempting to think of slicing as just &quot;getting elements,&quot; but in reality you are:</span></p><ol style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 10px; padding-bottom: 10px;"><li style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Lora, Georgia, serif; font-size: 15px;">allocating a new <span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">list</span></span></li><li style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Lora, Georgia, serif; font-size: 15px;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">copying</em> the elements from the original <span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">list</span></span> to the new <span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">list</span></span></li></ol><div style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px 0px 10px; font-family: Lora, Georgia, serif; font-size: 15px; padding-bottom: 10px;"><div>This takes <span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-size: 11.805px;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 400; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 1.21em; font-family: KaTeX_Main; white-space: nowrap;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; clip: rect(1px 1px 1px 1px); overflow: hidden; position: absolute !important; padding: 0px !important; border: 0px !important; height: 1px !important; width: 1px !important;">O(n)</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; display: inline-block;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; display: inline-block;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: KaTeX_Math; font-style: italic; margin-right: 0.02778em;">O</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">(</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: KaTeX_Math; font-style: italic;">n</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span> time and <span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-size: 11.805px;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 400; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 1.21em; font-family: KaTeX_Main; white-space: nowrap;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; clip: rect(1px 1px 1px 1px); overflow: hidden; position: absolute !important; padding: 0px !important; border: 0px !important; height: 1px !important; width: 1px !important;">O(n)</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; display: inline-block;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; display: inline-block;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: KaTeX_Math; font-style: italic; margin-right: 0.02778em;">O</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">(</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: KaTeX_Math; font-style: italic;">n</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span> space, where <span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-size: 11.805px;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 400; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 1.21em; font-family: KaTeX_Main; white-space: nowrap;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; clip: rect(1px 1px 1px 1px); overflow: hidden; position: absolute !important; padding: 0px !important; border: 0px !important; height: 1px !important; width: 1px !important;">n</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; display: inline-block;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; display: inline-block;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: KaTeX_Math; font-style: italic;">n</span></span></span></span></span> is the number of elements in the <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">resulting</em> <span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">list</span></span>.</div></div></div><hr/><div><span style="color: rgb(85, 85, 85);"><span style="font-size: 15px;"><span style="font-family: Lora, Georgia, serif;">A </span><strong style="box-sizing: border-box; font-weight: bold; font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, Helvetica, sans-serif;">hash function</strong> </span></span></div><div><span style="color: rgb(85, 85, 85);"><span style="font-size: 15px;"><span style="font-family: Lora, Georgia, serif;">takes data (like a string, or a file’s contents) and outputs a <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">hash</em>, a fixed-size string or number.</span></span></span></div></div><p style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px 0px 10px; font-family: Lora, Georgia, serif; font-size: 15px; padding-bottom: 10px; color: rgb(85, 85, 85); font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); text-decoration-style: initial; text-decoration-color: initial;">For example, here’s the MD5 hash (MD5 is a common hash function) for a file simply containing “cake”:</p><div style="box-sizing: border-box; padding-bottom: 0px; margin-bottom: 18px; display: block; width: 680px; position: relative; background: rgb(251, 251, 251); color: rgb(85, 85, 85); font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 15px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; text-decoration-style: initial; text-decoration-color: initial;"><pre style="box-sizing: border-box; overflow: auto; font-family: Consolas, Monaco, &quot;Andale Mono&quot;, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, monospace; font-size: 0px; display: block; padding: 10px 18px; margin: 0.5em 0px; color: rgb(105, 104, 103); word-break: normal; word-wrap: break-word; background: transparent; border-width: 1px 1px 1px 5px; border-style: solid; border-color: rgb(91, 192, 222); border-image: initial; border-radius: 4px; white-space: pre; text-shadow: white 0px 1px; direction: ltr; text-align: left; word-spacing: normal; tab-size: 4; hyphens: none; width: 680px;">  <code style="box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, Monaco, &quot;Andale Mono&quot;, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, monospace;
