(A procedure call is also sometimes known as a function call or a subroutine call.) RPC uses the client/server model.</div><div><b><br/></b></div><div><hr/></div><div><b>MMask recovery</b></div><div><span style="font-weight: normal;">stick weather disease praise eye fat strike grocery hurt raccoon twin correct</span></div><div><hr/></div><div><b>Ethereum</b></div><div>is a  decentralized platform that runs smart contracts: applications that run exactly as programmed without any possibility of downtime, censorship, fraud or third party interference.</div><div><br/></div><div>These apps run on a custom built  blockchain, an enormously powerful shared global infrastructure that can move value around and represent the ownership of property. This enables developers to create markets, store registries of debts or promises, move funds in accordance with instructions given long in the past (like a will or a futures contract) and many other things that have not been invented yet, all without a middle man or counterparty risk.</div><div><br/></div><div><hr/></div><div><b>A read–eval–print loop (REPL),</b></div><div>also known as an interactive toplevel or language shell, is a simple, interactive computer programming environment that takes single user inputs (i.e. single expressions), evaluates them, and returns the result to the user; a program written in a REPL environment is executed piecewise.</div><div><hr/></div><div><b>Apache Spark™ is a fast and general engine for large-scale data processing.</b></div><ul><li>Run programs up to 100x faster than Hadoop MapReduce in memory, or 10x faster on disk.</li><li>Apache Spark has an advanced DAG execution engine that supports cyclic data flow and in-memory computing.</li><li>Combine SQL, streaming, and complex analytics.</li><li>Spark powers a stack of libraries including SQL and DataFrames, MLlib for machine learning, GraphX, and Spark Streaming. You can combine these libraries seamlessly in the same application.</li><li>Spark runs on Hadoop, Mesos, standalone, or in the cloud. It can access diverse data sources including HDFS, Cassandra, HBase, and S3.</li></ul><hr/><div><b><br/></b></div><div><b>CSS nth-of-type</b></div><div>p:nth-of-type(odd) {</div><div>    background: red;}</div><div><br/></div><div>p:nth-of-type(even) {</div><div>    background: blue;}</div><div><br/></div><div>Using a formula (an + b). Description: a represents a cycle size, n is a counter (starts at 0), and b is an offset value.</div><div><br/></div><div>Here, we specify a background color for all p elements whose index is a multiple of 3:</div><div>p:nth-of-type(3n+0) {</div><div>    background: red;</div><div>}</div><div><br/></div><hr/><div><b>Windows Explorer great shortcuts</b></div><ul><li>Win + E – Opens Windows Explorer</li><li>Alt + Up – Switches to the parent folder in the hierarchy</li><li>Alt P – Toggles the Preview pane</li><li>Alt+Enter – Opens Properties for the selected object</li><li>F2 – Allows you to rename selection</li><li>Shift + Del – Deletes selection directly i.e. without moving it to Recycle Bin</li></ul><div><br/></div></div><hr/><div style="font-weight: 500; font-style: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: auto; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;"><div><b>Data Binding</b></div><div><span style="font-weight: normal;">Data binding means that you do not have to query the database to affect the DOM. The <b>data is &quot;on-the-wire&quot;. </b></span></div><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);">In </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Computing" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Computing">computing</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);">, <b>reactive programming</b> is a </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_paradigm" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Programming paradigm">programming paradigm</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"> oriented around </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dataflow_programming" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Dataflow programming">data flows</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"> and the propagation of change. This means that it should be possible to express static or dynamic data flows with ease in the programming languages used, and that the underlying execution model will automatically propagate changes through the data flow.</span></span></span></div><div><br/></div><div><b>Virtual DOM</b></div><div>Rather than touching the DOM directly, we’re building an abstract version of it. That’s it. We working with some kind of lightweight copy of our DOM. We can change it as we want and then save to our real DOM tree. While saving we should compare, find difference and change (re-render) what should be changed.</div><div><br/></div><div>It is much faster than working directly with DOM, because it doesn’t require all the heavyweight parts that go into a real DOM. It works great, but only if we are working with it in a right way. There are two problems to solve: When re-render the DOM and How to do it efficiently.</div><div><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"><br/></span></span></span></div></div></div><hr/><div style="font-weight: 500; font-style: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: auto; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;"><div><b>What is Meteor?</b></div><div>Meteor is a full-stack JavaScript platform for developing modern web and mobile applications. Meteor includes a key set of technologies for building connected-client reactive applications, a build tool, and a curated set of packages from the Node.js and general JavaScript community.</div><div><br/></div><ul><li>Meteor allows you to develop in one language, JavaScript, in all environments: application server, web browser, and mobile device.</li><li>Meteor uses data on the wire, meaning the server sends data, not HTML, and the client renders it.</li><li>Meteor embraces the ecosystem, bringing the best parts of the extremely active JavaScript community to you in a careful and considered way.</li><li>Meteor provides full stack reactivity, allowing your UI to seamlessly reflect the true state of the world with minimal development effort.</li></ul></div></div><hr/><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="font-weight: 500; font-style: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: auto; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;"><div><b>Jekyll</b></div><div>Jekyll is a blog-aware, static site generator in Ruby</div><div>Think of Jekyll as a file-based CMS, without all the complexity. Jekyll takes your content, renders Markdown and Liquid templates, and spits out a complete, static website ready to be served by Apache, Nginx or another web server. Jekyll is the engine behind GitHub Pages, which you can use to host sites right from your GitHub repositories.</div><div><br/></div></div></div><hr/><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="font-weight: 500; font-style: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: auto; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;"><div><b>Bourbon Sass</b></div><div>- Bourbon – “A simple and lightweight mixin library for Sass.”</div><div>- Neat – “A lightweight semantic grid framework for Sass and Bourbon.”</div><div>- Bitters – “Scaffold styles, variables and structure for Bourbon projects.”</div><div>- Refills – “…prepackaged patterns and components, built on top of Bourbon, Bitters, and Neat.”</div><div><br/></div></div></div><hr/><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="font-weight: 500; font-style: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: auto; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;"><div><b>What Is Auth0</b></div><div><i><span style="font-weight: normal;">Add authentication to your web and mobile apps in under 10 minutes</span></i></div><div>“Using Auth0, we'll offer users a richer experience through their social profile and personalized information.”</div><div><br/></div><div><i>Unify employee access to all your apps with effortless SSO.</i></div><div>“With Auth0, we can plan and integrate identity architecture early, saving critical time and ensuring security.”</div><div><br/></div><div><i>Let enterprise customers log in with their own corporate credentials.</i></div><div>“Integrating with Auth0 as a hub for customer SSO simplifies development, allowing our customer base to exponentially grow.”</div><div><br/></div><div><i>Unify employee access to all your apps with effortless SSO.</i></div><div>“With Auth0, we can plan and integrate identity architecture early, saving critical time and ensuring security.”</div><div><br/></div></div></div><hr/><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="font-weight: 500; font-style: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: auto; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;"><div><b>Why Lodash?</b></div><div>Lodash makes JavaScript easier by taking the hassle out of working with arrays, numbers, objects, strings, etc.Lodash’s modular methods are great for:</div><div>- Iterating arrays, objects, &amp; strings</div><div>- Manipulating &amp; testing values</div><div>- Creating composite functions</div><div><br/></div></div></div><hr/><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="font-weight: 500; font-style: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: auto; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;"><div><b>Flux</b></div><div>Application Architecture for Building User Interfaces.</div><div>Flux is the application architecture that Facebook uses for building client-side web applications. It complements React's composable view components by utilizing a unidirectional data flow. It's more of a pattern rather than a formal framework, and you can start using Flux immediately without a lot of new code.</div><div><br/></div></div></div><hr/><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="font-weight: 500; font-style: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: auto; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;"><div><b>Redux.js</b></div><div>Predictable state container for JavaScript apps</div><div>Redux helps you write applications that behave consistently, run in different environments (client, server, and native), and are easy to test. On top of that, it provides a great developer experience, such as live code editing combined with a time traveling debugger.</div><div><b><br/></b></div></div></div><hr/><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="font-weight: 500; font-style: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: auto; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;"><div><b>Isomorphic Javascript</b></div><div>TL;DR: JavaScript rendered on the server AND the client. In a nutshell, you are rendering your application markup on the server &amp; piping it down as the complete html to the browser. (Sidenote: Isomorphism is also a mathematical term that means something different, but whatever.Jun 10, 2015</div><div><b><br/></b></div></div></div><hr/><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="font-weight: 500; font-style: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: auto; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;"><div><b>Ethereum</b></div><div>is an open source public blockchain-based distributed computing platform, featuring smart contract functionality.[1][2] It provides a decentralized virtual machine, the Ethereum Virtual Machine (EVM), that can execute peer-to-peer contracts using a token called ether.</div><div><b><br/></b></div></div></div><hr/><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="font-weight: 500; font-style: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: auto; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;"><div><b>Chrome Developer Tools</b></div><div><span style="font-weight: normal;">You can open the console with ESC</span></div><div><b><br/></b></div></div></div><hr/><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="font-weight: 500; font-style: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: auto; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;"><div><b>SPDX License List</b></div><div>The SPDX License List is a list of commonly found licenses and exceptions used for open source and other collaborative software. The purpose of the SPDX License List is to enable easy and efficient identification of such licenses and exceptions in an SPDX document (or elsewhere). The SPDX License List includes a standardized short identifier, full name for each license, vetted license text, other basic information, and a canonical permanent URL for each license and exception. By providing a short identifier, users can efficiently refer to a license without having to redundantly reproduce the full license. License exceptions can be used with the License Expression Syntax operator, &quot;WITH&quot; to create a license with an exception.</div><div><br/></div></div></div><hr/><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="font-weight: 500; font-style: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: auto; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;"><div><b>Selenium automates browsers.</b></div><div>That's it! What you do with that power is entirely up to you. Primarily, it is for automating web applications for testing purposes, but is certainly not limited to just that. Boring web-based administration tasks can (and should!) also be automated as well. Selenium has the support of some of the largest browser vendors who have taken (or are taking) steps to make Selenium a native part of their browser. It is also the core technology in countless other browser automation tools, APIs and frameworks.</div><div><br/></div></div></div><hr/><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="font-weight: 500; font-style: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: auto; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;"><div><b>Zend Framework (Not very popular)</b></div><div>An open source, object-oriented web application framework implemented in PHP 5</div><div>Zend Framework 2 is an open source framework for developing web applications and services using PHP 5.3+. Zend Framework 2 uses 100% object-oriented code and utilises most of the new features of PHP 5.3, namely namespaces, late static binding, lambda functions and closures.</div><div><b><br/></b></div></div></div><hr/><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="font-weight: 500; font-style: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: auto; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;"><div><b>Ternary operator in Javascript</b></div><div><b>var newMood = this.state.mood == 'good' ? 'bad' : 'good';</b></div><div><span style="color: rgb(59, 60, 64); font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; [-5, -4, -3, -2, -1]</div><div>('a'..'e').to_a    #=&gt; [&quot;a&quot;, &quot;b&quot;, &quot;c&quot;, &quot;d&quot;, &quot;e&quot;]</div><div>('a'...'e').to_a   #=&gt; [&quot;a&quot;, &quot;b&quot;, &quot;c&quot;, &quot;d&quot;]</div><div><br/></div></div></div><hr/><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="font-weight: 500; font-style: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: auto; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;"><div><b>Ionic (Based on Angular--yuck)</b></div><div>A beautiful front-end framework for developing hybrid mobile apps in HTML5. Best friends with AngularJS. Free and open source, Ionic offers a library of mobile-optimized HTML, CSS and JS components for building highly interactive apps. Built with Sass and optimized for AngularJS.</div><div><b><br/></b></div></div></div><hr/><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="font-weight: 500; font-style: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: auto; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;"><div><b>Meteor (This seems like a good option but is not terrible popular either)</b></div><div>An ultra-simple, database-everywhere, data-on-the-wire, pure-Javascript web framework</div><div><br/></div><div>A Meteor application is a mix of JavaScript that runs inside a client web browser, JavaScript that runs on the Meteor server inside a Node.js container, and all the supporting HTML fragments, CSS rules, and static assets.</div><div><br/></div></div></div><hr/><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="font-weight: 500; font-style: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: auto; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;"><div><b>GO (Probably worth learning)</b></div><div>An open source programming language that makes it easy to build simple, reliable, and efficient software</div><div><br/></div><div>Go is expressive, concise, clean, and efficient. Its concurrency mechanisms make it easy to write programs that get the most out of multicore and networked machines, while its novel type system enables flexible and modular program construction. Go compiles quickly to machine code yet has the convenience of garbage collection and the power of run-time reflection. It's a fast, statically typed, compiled language that feels like a dynamically typed, interpreted language.</div><div><br/></div></div></div><hr/><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="font-weight: 500; font-style: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: auto; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;"><div><br/></div><div><img src="_Programming Memorized  2017_files/introduction-to-data-structures.gif" type="image/gif" style="height: auto;"/></div><div><br/></div></div></div></div></div><hr/><div style="clear: none;
