font-style: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="font-weight: normal;"><br/></div><div style="font-weight: normal;"><b>headless browser</b></div><div style="font-weight: normal;">is a web browser without a graphical user interface. Headlessbrowsers provide automated control of a web page in an environment similar to popular web browsers, but are executed via a command-line interface or using network communication.</div><div style="font-weight: normal;"><br/></div><div style="font-weight: normal;"><b>PhantomJS</b></div><div style="font-weight: normal;">is a headless WebKit scriptable with a JavaScript API. It has fast and native support for various web standards: DOM handling, CSS selector, JSON, Canvas, and SVG.</div><div style="font-weight: normal;"><br/></div><div style="font-weight: normal;"><b>Jekyll</b></div><div style="font-weight: normal;">is a simple, blog-aware, static site generator for personal, project, or organization sites. </div><div style="font-weight: normal;">Instead of using databases, Jekyll takes the content, renders Markdown or Textile and Liquid templates,[4] and produces a complete, static website ready to be served by Apache HTTP Server, Nginx or another web server.[5] Jekyll is the engine behind GitHub Pages. Jekyll is flexible and supports front-end frameworks such as Bootstrap,[7] Semantic UI and many others.</div><div style="font-weight: normal;"><br/></div><div style="font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Verdana, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 12.96px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); display: inline !important; float: none;"><b>Apache Ant</b></span></div><div style="font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Verdana, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 12.96px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); display: inline !important; float: none;">is a Java library and command-line tool whose mission is to drive processes described in build files as targets and extension points dependent upon each other. The main known usage of Ant is the build of Java applications. Ant supplies a number of built-in tasks allowing to compile, assemble, test and run Java applications. Ant can also be used effectively to build non Java applications, for instance C or C++ applications. More generally, Ant can be used to pilot any type of process which can be described in terms of targets and tasks.</span></div><div style="font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-size: 16.5px;"><span style="font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', HelveticaNeue, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><br/></span></span></span></span></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><hr/><div style="margin: 0px 0px 0.7em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: normal; font-stretch: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0px 0px 0.7em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: normal; font-stretch: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0px 0px 5px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; width: 660px; word-wrap: break-word; padding: 0px; border: 0px; clear: both;"><div style="clear: none; padding: 10px 16px; font-style: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="overflow: hidden; padding-bottom: 20px;"><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="box-sizing: border-box; font-style: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="font-weight: normal;"><b>Immutable</b></div><div style="font-weight: normal;">Immutable data cannot be changed once created, leading to much simpler application development, no defensive copying, and enabling advanced memoization and change detection techniques with simple logic. Persistent data presents a mutative API which does not update the data in-place, but instead always yields new updated data.</div><div style="font-weight: normal;"><br/></div><div style="font-weight: normal;"><b>Memoization</b></div><div style="font-weight: normal;">In computing, memoization or memoisation is an optimization technique used primarily to speed up computer programs by storing the results of expensive function calls and returning the cached result when the same inputs occur again.</div><div style="font-weight: normal;"><br/></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><hr/><div style="margin: 0px 0px 0.7em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: normal; font-stretch: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0px 0px 0.7em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: normal; font-stretch: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0px 0px 5px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; width: 660px; word-wrap: break-word; font-style: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; clear: both;"><div style="clear: none; padding: 10px 16px; font-style: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="overflow: hidden; padding-bottom: 20px;"><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="box-sizing: border-box; font-style: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-size: 21px;"><b>Software-defined networking (SDN)</b></span></div><div style="font-weight: normal;">is an approach to computer networking that allows network administrators to manage network services through abstraction of lower-level functionality. SDN is meant to address the fact that the static architecture of traditional networks doesn't support the dynamic, scalable computing and storage needs of more modern computing environments such as data centers</div><div style="font-weight: normal;"><b><br/></b></div><div style="font-weight: normal;"><b>CoreOS</b><br/></div><div style="font-weight: normal;">is a powerful Linux distribution built to make large, scalable deployments on varied infrastructure simple to manage. Based on a build of Chrome OS, CoreOSmaintains a lightweight host system and uses Docker containers for all applications.</div><div style="font-weight: normal;"><br/></div><div style="font-weight: normal;"><b>Kubernetes</b><br/></div><div style="font-weight: normal;">(commonly referred to as &quot;k8s&quot;) is an open source container cluster manager originally designed by Google and donated to the Cloud Native Computing Foundation. It aims to provide a &quot;platform for automating deployment, scaling, and operations of application containers across clusters of hosts&quot;.</div><div style="font-weight: normal;"><br/></div><div style="font-weight: normal;"><b>Etcd</b></div><div style="font-weight: normal;">One of the fundamental components that Kubernetes needs to function is a globally available configuration store. The etcd project, developed by the CoreOS team, is a lightweight, distributed key-value store that can be distributed across multiple nodes.</div><div style="font-weight: normal;"><br/></div><div style="font-weight: normal;"><b>Docker</b></div><div style="font-weight: normal;">is an open-source project that automates the deployment of Linux applications inside software containers. Quote of features from Docker web pages: ...Docker provides an additional layer of abstraction and automation of operating-system-level virtualization on Linux.</div><div style="font-weight: normal;"><br/></div><div style="font-weight: normal;"><b>CoreOS, Apache Mesos</b>, <b>Mesosphere, </b><b>DC/OS</b></div><div style="font-weight: normal;">Data Center Operating Systems</div><div style="font-weight: normal;"><br/></div><div style="font-weight: normal;"><b>Kubernetes</b>, <b>Swarm</b>, <b>Marathon</b>, <b>Rancher</b></div><div style="font-weight: normal;">Container Orchastration Engines</div><div style="font-weight: normal;"><br/></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><hr style="font-weight: normal;"/><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0px 0px 0.7em; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0px 0px 0.7em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; margin-left: 40px;"><b>Apache Chronos</b> is the “cron” for your <b>Mesosphere DC/OS</b>. It is a highly-available distributed job scheduler, providing the most robust way to run batch jobs in your datacenter. Chronos schedules jobs across the <b>Mesos</b> cluster and manages dependencies between jobs in an intelligent way.</div><div style="font-weight: normal; margin-left: 40px;"><b>Apache Aurora</b> is a <b>Mesosphere</b> framework for long-running services and cron jobs.</div><div style="font-weight: normal; margin-left: 40px;"><b>Metronome</b>: Cron Service for DC/OS</div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><hr style="font-weight: normal;"/><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0px 0px 0.7em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; clear: both;"><div style="clear: none; padding: 10px 16px; font-style: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="overflow: hidden; padding-bottom: 20px;"><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="box-sizing: border-box; font-style: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-size: 17px;"><b>LOL, just use what works for you.</b></span></div><div style="font-weight: normal;">&quot;Right now, I have a near frictionless CSS workflow. I write in Sass, compile with Libsass and get vendor prefixes added with PostCSS/Autoprefixer via Gulp/Grunt. Why would I want to upset that?&quot;</div><div style="font-weight: normal;"><b><br/></b></div><div style="font-weight: normal;"><b>SMACSS—Scalable and Modular Architecture for CSS</b></div><div style="font-weight: normal;">It's a book and a methodology for writing CSS (created by Jonathan Snook), but its most significant and influential aspect is its organizational system, which is designed to provide a set of buckets into which CSS should be organized.</div><div style="font-weight: normal;"><b><br/></b></div><div style="font-weight: normal;"><b>Object oriented CSS (OOCSS)</b></div><div style="font-weight: normal;">is a methodology of writing reusable CSS that is fast, scalable and maintainable. It’s the first of the popular CSS “systems” (SMACSS &amp; BEM are two other popular systems) that aim at making CSS more modular and scaleable.</div><div style="font-weight: normal;"><br/></div><div style="font-weight: normal;"><b>Atomic CSS (ACSS)</b></div><div style="font-weight: normal;">Atoms (input), Molecules (label, input, button), Organisms (Set of molecules, e.g. a header, Templates (Wireframe), Pages (actual site with data &amp; images.</div><div style="font-weight: normal;"><br/></div><div style="font-weight: normal;"><b>Harp</b></div><div style="font-weight: normal;">The static web server with built-in preprocessing.</div><div style="font-weight: normal;">Harp serves Jade, Markdown, EJS, CoffeeScript, Sass, LESS and Stylus as HTML, CSS &amp; JavaScript—no configuration necessary. Harpautomatically preprocesses code and serves it to the browser as HTML, CSS, and JavaScript. Now you can focus on writing instead of wrangling.</div><div style="font-weight: normal;"><br/></div><div style="font-weight: normal;"><b>PostCSS</b></div><div style="font-weight: normal;">is a tool for transforming styles with JS plugins. These plugins can lint your CSS, support variables and mixins, transpile future CSS syntax, inline images, and more.PostCSS is used by industry leaders including Wikipedia, Twitter, Alibaba, and JetBrains.</div><div style="font-weight: normal;"><br/></div><div style="font-weight: normal;"><b>Handlebars.js</b></div><div style="font-weight: normal;">This is a complete tutorial, and indeed a reference, on Handlebars.js templating and, principally, JavaScript templating.Handlebars.js is a client-side (though it can be used on the server, too) templating engine for </div><div style="font-weight: normal;"><br/></div><div style="font-weight: normal;"><a href="http://clubmate.fi/oocss-acss-bem-smacss-what-are-they-what-should-i-use/">http://clubmate.fi/oocss-acss-bem-smacss-what-are-they-what-should-i-use/</a></div><div style="font-weight: normal;"><br/></div><div style="font-weight: normal; display: block; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Tahoma; font-size: medium; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;"><b>Test-driven development (TDD)</b></div><div style="font-weight: normal; display: block; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-size: medium; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;"><div>is a software development process that relies on the repetition of a very short development cycle: requirements are turned into very specific test cases, then the software is improved to pass the new tests, only. <span style="font-size: medium;">&quot;Test-first fundamentalism is like abstinence-only sex ed: An unrealistic, ineffective morality campaign for self-loathing and shaming.&quot;</span></div></div><div style="font-weight: normal; display: block; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;"><div><br/></div><div><b>Redux</b></div><div>is a predictable state container for JavaScript apps. (If you're looking for a WordPress framework, check out Redux Framework.) It helps you write applications that behave consistently, run in different environments (client, server, and native), and are easy to test. On top of that, it provides a great developer experience, such as live code editing combined with a time traveling debugger.</div></div><div style="font-weight: normal;"><br/></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><hr style="font-weight: normal;"/><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0px 0px 0.7em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: normal; font-stretch: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0px 0px 0.7em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: normal; font-stretch: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0px 0px 5px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; width: 660px; word-wrap: break-word; font-style: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; clear: both;"><div style="clear: none; padding: 10px 16px; font-style: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="overflow: hidden; padding-bottom: 20px;"><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="box-sizing: border-box; font-style: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="font-weight: normal;"><b>Web Components</b></div><div style="font-weight: normal;">consists of several separate technologies. You can think of Web Components as reusable user interface widgets that are created using open Web technology. They are part of the browser, and so they do not need external libraries like jQuery or Dojo. An existing Web Component can be used without writing code, simply by adding an import statement to an HTML page. Web Components use new or still-developing standard browser capabilities.<br/></div><div style="font-weight: normal;"><b><br/></b></div><div style="font-weight: normal;"><b>RamdaJS, UnderscoreJS, lodash</b></div><div style="font-weight: normal;">FUNCTIONAL PROGRAMMING JS LIBRARIES (e.g. sorting data)</div><div style="font-weight: normal;">Ramda is very like underscore and lodash, but there are some cool differences.</div><div style="font-weight: normal;"><br/></div><div style="font-weight: normal;"><b>KnockoutJS</b></div><div style="font-weight: normal;">is basically a library written in JavaScript that is based on MVVM pattern that helps developers building rich and responsive websites. This separates the application's Model (stored data), View (UI) and View Model (JavascriptRepresentation of model). KO is an abbreviation used for KnockoutJS.</div><div style="font-weight: normal;"><b><br/></b></div><div style="font-weight: normal;"><b>Progressive web apps</b></div><div style="font-weight: normal;">Progressive web apps could be the next big thing for the mobile web. Originally proposed by Google in 2015, they have already attracted a lot of attention because of the relative ease of development and the almost instant wins for the application’s user experience.</div><div style="font-weight: normal;"><b><br/></b></div><div style="font-weight: normal;"><b>AMP</b></div><div style="font-weight: normal;">Accelerated Mobile Pages </div><div style="font-weight: normal;"><b><br/></b></div><div style="font-weight: normal;"><b>What is a service worker?</b></div><div style="font-weight: normal;">A service worker is a script that your browser runs in the background, separate from a web page, opening the door to features that don't need a web page or user interaction. Today, they already include features like push notifications and background sync. In the future service workers will support other things like periodic sync or geofencing. </div><div style="font-weight: normal;"><b><br/></b></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><hr style="font-weight: normal;"/><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; For POSIX-like machines, the shell provisioner executes scripts with SSH. For Windows guest machines that are configured to use WinRM, the shell provisioner executes PowerShell and Batch scripts over WinRM.</div><div style="font-weight: normal;"><br/></div><div style="font-weight: normal;"><b>Posix</b></div><div style="font-weight: normal;">- a set of formal descriptions that provide a standard for the design of operating systems, especially ones that are compatible with Unix.</div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><hr style="font-weight: normal;"/><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; Underscore provides over 100 functions that support both your favorite workaday functional helpers: map, filter, invoke — as well as more specialized goodies: function binding, javascript templating, creating quick indexes, deep equality testing, and so on.</div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><hr style="font-weight: normal;"/><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; (JS utility library)</b></div><div style="font-weight: normal;">Lodash makes JavaScript easier by taking the hassle out of working with arrays, numbers, objects, strings, etc.Lodash’s modular methods are great for:</div><div style="font-weight: normal;"><br/></div><div style="font-weight: normal;">- Iterating arrays, objects, &amp; (Ternary (Inline Conditional)) Operator</b></div><div style="font-weight: normal;">In computer programming, ?: is a ternary operator that is part of the syntax for a basic conditional expression in several programming languages. It is commonly referred to as the conditional operator, inline if (iif), or ternary if.</div><div style="font-weight: normal;"><br/></div><div style="font-weight: normal;"><i>?: is used as follows:</i></div><div style="font-weight: normal;">condition ? value_if_true : value_if_false</div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><hr style="font-weight: normal;"/><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px;   &lt;input<br/>
    class=&quot;form__submit form__submit--disabled&quot;<br/>
    type=&quot;submit&quot; /&gt;<br/>
&lt;/form&gt;<br/><br/></div><div style="font-weight: normal;"><br/></div><div style="font-weight: normal;">CSS</div><div style="font-weight: normal;">.form { }</div><div style="font-weight: normal;">.form--theme-xmas { }</div><div style="font-weight: normal;">.form--simple { }</div><div style="font-weight: normal;">.form__input { }</div><div style="font-weight: normal;">.form__submit { }</div><div style="font-weight: normal;">.form__submit--disabled { }</div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><hr style="font-weight: normal;"/><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; font-stretch: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0px 0px 5px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; width: 660px; word-wrap: break-word; font-style: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; clear: both;"><div style="clear: none; padding: 10px 16px; font-style: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="overflow: hidden; padding-bottom: 20px;"><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37); font-family: sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); display: inline !important; float: none;">A </span><b style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37); font-family: sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">read–eval–print loop</b><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37); font-family: sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); display: inline !important; float: none;"> (</span><b style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37); font-family: sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">REPL</b><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37); font-family: sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); display: inline !important; float: none;">), also known as an </span><b style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37); font-family: sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">interactive toplevel</b><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37); font-family: sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); display: inline !important; float: none;"> or </span><b style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37); font-family: sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">language shell</b><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37); font-family: sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); display: inline !important; float: none;">, is a simple, interactive </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Computer_programming" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none rgb(255, 255, 255); font-family: sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;" title="Computer programming">computer programming</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37); font-family: sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); display: inline !important; float: none;"> environment that takes single user inputs (i.e. single </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Expression_(computer_science)" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none rgb(255, 255, 255); font-family: sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;" title="Expression (computer science)">expressions</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37); font-family: sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); display: inline !important; float: none;">), evaluates them, and returns the result to the user; a program written in a REPL environment is executed piecewise. The term is most usually used to refer to programming interfaces similar to the classic </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lisp_machine" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none rgb(255, 255, 255); font-family: sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;" title="Lisp machine">Lisp machine</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37); font-family: sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); display: inline !important; float: none;"> interactive environment. Common examples include </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Command_line_interface" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none rgb(255, 255, 255); font-family: sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;" title="Command line interface">command line</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37); font-family: sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); display: inline !important; float: none;"> </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Shell_(computing)" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none rgb(255, 255, 255); font-family: sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;" title="Shell (computing)">shells</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37); font-family: sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); display: inline !important; float: none;"> and similar environments for </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_languages" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none rgb(255, 255, 255); font-family: sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;" title="Programming languages">programming languages</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37); font-family: sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); display: inline !important; float: none;">, and is particularly characteristic of </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scripting_language" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none rgb(255, 255, 255); font-family: sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;" title="Scripting language">scripting languages</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37); font-family: sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); display: inline !important; float: none;">.</span><sup style="unicode-bidi: isolate; white-space: nowrap; font-size: 11.2px; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal; color: rgb(37, 37, 37); font-family: sans-serif; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Read%E2%80%93eval%E2%80%93print_loop#cite_note-1" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none; white-space: nowrap;">[1]</a></sup></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><hr style="font-weight: normal;"/><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0px 0px 0.7em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: normal; font-stretch: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0px 0px 0.7em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: normal; font-stretch: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0px 0px 5px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; width: 660px; word-wrap: break-word; font-style: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; clear: both;"><div style="clear: none; padding: 10px 16px; font-style: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="overflow: hidden; padding-bottom: 20px;"><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: sans-serif;">In <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Computer_science" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Computer science">computer science</a>, <b>syntactic sugar</b> is <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Syntax_(programming_languages)" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Syntax (programming languages)">syntax</a> within a <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Programming language">programming language</a> that is designed to make things easier to read or to express. It makes the language &quot;sweeter&quot; for human use: things can be expressed more clearly, more concisely, or in an alternative style that some may prefer.</span></span></span></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><hr style="font-weight: normal;"/><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0px 0px 0.7em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: normal; font-stretch: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0px 0px 0.7em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: normal; font-stretch: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0px 0px 5px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; width: 660px; word-wrap: break-word; font-style: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; clear: both;"><div style="clear: none; padding: 10px 16px; font-style: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="overflow: hidden; padding-bottom: 20px;"><div style="font-weight: normal;"><b>What are callbacks?</b></div><div style="font-weight: normal;">Callbacks are just the name of a convention for using JavaScript functions. There isn't a special thing called a 'callback' in the JavaScript language, it's just a convention. Instead of immediately returning some result like most functions, functions that use callbacks take some time to produce a result. The word 'asynchronous', aka 'async' just means 'takes some time' or 'happens in the future, not right now'. Usually callbacks are only used when doing I/O, e.g. downloading things, reading files, talking to databases, etc. </div><div style="font-weight: normal;"><div><br/></div><div>When you call a normal function you can use its return value:</div><pre style="box-sizing: border-box; border: 1px solid rgb(213, 224, 228); word-wrap: normal; padding: 10px; margin-bottom: 20px; font-family: &quot;Bitstream Vera Sans Mono&quot;, Courier, monospace; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); background: rgb(248, 248, 248); border-radius: 3px; font-size: 13px; overflow: auto; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;"><code style="box-sizing: border-box; border: none; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-size: 12px; font-family: Menlo, monospace; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); background: rgb(248, 248, 248); border-radius: 3px;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-weight: bold;">var</span> result <span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-weight: bold;">=</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box;">multiplyTwoNumbers</span>(<span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-weight: normal; color: rgb(0, 153, 153);">5</span>, <span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-weight: normal; color: rgb(0, 153, 153);">10</span>)
console.<span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(0, 134, 179);">log</span>(result)
<span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(153, 153, 136);">// 50 gets printed out</span></code></pre><div style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-bottom: 20px; margin-top: 10px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;"><div>However, functions that are async and use callbacks don't return anything right away.</div></div><pre style="box-sizing: border-box; border: 1px solid rgb(213, 224, 228); word-wrap: normal; padding: 10px; margin-bottom: 20px; font-family: &quot;Bitstream Vera Sans Mono&quot;, Courier, monospace; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); background: rgb(248, 248, 248); border-radius: 3px; font-size: 13px; overflow: auto; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;"><code style="box-sizing: border-box; border: none; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-size: 12px; font-family: Menlo, monospace; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); background: rgb(248, 248, 248); border-radius: 3px;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-weight: bold;">var</span> photo <span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-weight: bold;">=</span> <span style="box-sizing: border-box;">downloadPhoto</span>(<span style="box-sizing: border-box; font-weight: normal; color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">'<a dir="ltr" href="http://coolcats.com/cat.gif">http://coolcats.com/cat.gif</a>'</span>)
<span style="box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(153, 153, 136);">// photo is 'undefined'!</span></code></pre><div style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-bottom: 20px; margin-top: 10px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;"><div>In this case the gif might take a very long time to download, and you don't want your program to pause (aka 'block') while waiting for the download to finish.</div><div><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: 'Open Sans', Arial, sans-serif;"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><span style="color: rgb(59, 60, 64);"><br/></span></span></span></span></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><hr/><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0px 0px 0.7em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: normal; font-stretch: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0px 0px 0.7em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: normal; font-stretch: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0px 0px 5px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; width: 660px; word-wrap: break-word; font-style: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; clear: both;"><div style="clear: none; padding: 10px 16px; font-style: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="overflow: hidden; padding-bottom: 20px;"><div style="font-weight: normal;"><div style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-bottom: 20px; margin-top: 10px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;"><div><b>Arrow Function</b></div><div>An arrow function expression has a shorter syntax compared to function expressions and does not bind its own this, arguments, super, or new.target. Arrow functions are always anonymous. These function expressions are best suited for non-method functions and they can not be used as constructors.</div><div><br/></div><div>Example</div><div>var a2 = a.map(function(s){ return s.length });</div><div>var a3 = a.map( s =&gt; s.length );</div><div><span style="font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: OpenSans, sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(87, 103, 110);"><br/></span></span></span></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><hr style="font-weight: normal;"/><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; The WebSocket protocol was standardized by the IETF as RFC 6455 in 2011, and the WebSocket API in Web IDL is being standardized by the W3C.</div><div><b><br/></b></div><div><b>XMLHttpRequest (XHR)</b></div><div>is an API available to web browser scripting languages such as JavaScript. It is used to send HTTP or HTTPS requests to a web server and load the server response data back into the script.</div><div><br/></div><div><b>Glob Patterns</b></div><div><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37); font-family: sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; clear: both;"><div><span style="font-size: 20px;"><b>JQuery Refresher</b></span></div><div><b>What is a Library?</b></div><div>jQuery is a library, or set of helpful add-ons, to the JavaScript programming language. It may seem counterintuitive to learn how to use a library before learning the actual language, but there are a few good reasons for this.</div><div><br/></div><div><b>Library vs Framework</b></div><div>- The key difference between a library and a framework is &quot;Inversion of Control&quot;. When you call a method from a library, you are in control. But with a framework, the control is inverted: the framework calls you. A library is just a collection of class definitions.</div><div><br/></div><div><strong style="font-weight: bold; box-sizing: border-box; -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, &quot;Hevetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 15px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">event handler</strong><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, &quot;Hevetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 15px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); display: inline !important; float: none;"> on an element—that's the fancy name for actions like </span><code style="box-sizing: border-box; -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); padding: 0.15em 0.25em; font-size: 0.85em; border-radius: 2px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.0470588); border: 1px solid rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.0666667); font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, Consolas, source-code-pro, monospace; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;">.click()</code><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, &quot;Hevetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, sans-serif; -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); padding: 0.15em 0.25em; font-size: 0.85em; border-radius: 2px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.0470588); border: 1px solid rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.0666667); font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, Consolas, source-code-pro, monospace;">.append()</code>, but it just reverses the order of &quot;what to add&quot; and &quot;where to add it.&quot; The code</p><div style="box-sizing: border-box; -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-color: rgb(35, 44, 49); color: rgb(197, 200, 198); border-radius: 2px; color: rgb(181, 189, 104);">'.info'</span>);</code></div></div><div><br/></div><div><b>Literal</b></div><div>In programming, a value written exactly as it's meant to be interpreted. In contrast, a variable is a name that can represent different values during the execution of the program. And a constant is a name that represents the same value throughout a program. But a literal is not a name -- it is the value itself.</div><div><br/></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><hr/><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;">if</code>/<code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;">else</code> statements make binary decisions and execute separate code based on a condition.We can add extra conditions with to <code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;">if</code>/<code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;">else</code> statements with <code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;">else if</code>conditions.<code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;">switch</code> statements make complicated <code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;">if</code>/<code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;">else</code> statements easier to read, however they achieve the same result as <code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;">if</code>/<code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;">else</code> statements.<em style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: italic; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box;">Comparison operators</em>, like <code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;">&lt;</code>, <code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;">&gt;</code>, <code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;">&lt;=</code>, and <code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;">&gt;=</code> can compare two variables. After they compare, they always return either <code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;">true</code> or <code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;">false</code>.<em style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: italic; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box;">Logical Operators</em>, like <code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;">&amp;&amp;</code>, <code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;">||</code>, <code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;">!==</code>, and <code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;">!</code>, can compare two variables to see if a certain condition exists:
<ul style="margin: 0.5em 0px 0.7em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; list-style: none;"><li><code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;">&amp;&amp;</code> checks if both sides are <code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;">true</code>.<code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;">||</code> checks if either side is <code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;">true</code>.<code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;">!==</code> checks if both sides are not equal.<code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;">!</code> changes a variable that is <code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;">true</code> to <code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;">false</code>, and vice versa.</li></ul></li></ul><div style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: 300; font-stretch: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 64);"><span style="font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: Oxygen, Oxygen, 'Segoe UI', 'Helvetica Neue', sans-serif;">In the next lesson, we'll learn about functions, and how to write blocks of code that are reusable.</span></span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: Oxygen, Oxygen, 'Segoe UI', 'Helvetica Neue', sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 64);"><br/></span></span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: Oxygen, Oxygen, 'Segoe UI', 'Helvetica Neue', sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 64);"><em style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: italic; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box;"><b>Scope</b></em></span></span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: Oxygen, Oxygen, 'Segoe UI', 'Helvetica Neue', sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 64);">is the idea in programming that some variables are acessible/inaccessible from other parts of the program.<em style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: italic; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box;">Global Scope</em> refers to variables that are accessible to every part of the program.<em style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: italic; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box;">Functional Scope</em> refers to variables created inside functions, which are not accessible outside of its block.</span></span></span></div><div><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 64);"><span style="font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: Oxygen, Oxygen, 'Segoe UI', 'Helvetica Neue', sans-serif;"><br/></span></span></span></div><div><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 64);"><span style="font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: Oxygen, Oxygen, 'Segoe UI', 'Helvetica Neue', sans-serif;"><b>Basic JS Function Operation and Nesting Example</b></span></span></span></div><div>var orderCount = 0;</div><div>var takeOrder = function(topping, crustType) {</div><div>  orderCount ++;</div><div>  console.log('Order: ' + crustType + ' crust pizza topped with ' + topping );</div><div>};</div><div><br/></div><div>var getSubTotal = function(itemCount) {</div><div>  return itemCount * 7.5;</div><div>};</div><div><br/></div><div>var getTax = function() {</div><div>  return getSubTotal(orderCount) * (0.06);</div><div>};</div><div><br/></div><div>var getTotal = function() {</div><div>  return getSubTotal(orderCount) + getTax();</div><div>};</div><div><br/></div><div>takeOrder('bacon', 'thin');</div><div>takeOrder('pepperoni', 'regular');</div><div>takeOrder('sausage', 'pan');</div><div>console.log(getTotal());</div></div></div><div><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 64);"> </span></div><div><b><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 64);">JS While Loop currentCard = cards[randomNumber];</span></div><div><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 64);">};</span></div><div><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 64);">if (currentCard === 'Spade') {</span></div><div><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 64);">    console.log('You found a ' + currentCard + '!');</span></div><div><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 64);">};</span></div><div><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 64);"><br/></span></div><div><b><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 64);">JS For Loop Example</span></b></div><div><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 64);">var myPlaces = console.log(myPlaces[i]);</span></div><div><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 64);">  for (var j = 0; j &lt; friendPlaces.length; j++){</span></div><div><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 64);">    if &quot;!&quot;);</span></div><div><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 64);">    };</span></div><div><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 64);">  };</span></div><div><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; clear: both;"><div><b>Memory leaks</b></div><div>are a class of bugs where the application fails to release memorywhen no longer needed. Over time, memory leaks affect the performance of both the particular application as well as the operating system. A large leak might result in unacceptable response times due to excessive paging. <br/></div><div><b><br/></b></div><div><b>Garbage Collection</b></div><div>Low-level languages, like C, have low-level memory management primitives like malloc() and free() . On the other hand, JavaScript values are allocated when things (objects, strings, etc.) are created and &quot;automatically&quot; freed when they are not used anymore. The latter process is called garbage collection.</div><div><b><br/></b></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><hr/><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0px 0px 0.7em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: 300; font-stretch: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; padding: 0px; border: 0px; clear: both;"><div><span style="font-size: 23px;"><b>2016 CSS/HTML Front End Refresher</b></span></div></div><div style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; clear: both;"><div><b>Emojis and Fonts</b></div><div>Emojis are part of the Unicode Spec--Meaning they can be invoked in plain text but are MISSING FROM MANY FONTS. So, user input fields that may contain emojis should be Considered.</div><div>Below is are histograms and box charts showing people's different reactions to both specific emojis, and emojis that display differently in different contexts.</div><div><img src="_Programming Memorized  2017_files/Image [9].png" type="image/png" style="height: auto;"/><img src="_Programming Memorized  2017_files/Image [10].png" type="image/png" style="height: auto;"/><br/></div><div><span style="font-size: 17px;"><b>Viewport Relative Units</b></span></div><div>vw: 1/100th viewport width</div><div>vh: 1/100th viewport height</div><div>vmin: 1/100th of the smallest side</div><div>vmax: 1/100th of the largest side</div><div><br/></div><div><span style="font-size: 17px;"><b>CSS3 Calc Use Cases</b></span></div><div>div {</div><div>   font-size:<b> calc(3em + 5px)</b>; /* combine units */</div><div>   padding: <b>calc(1vmax + -1vmin);</b> /* useful for defining relative to viewport, for example fluid text sizes */</div><div>   transform: rotate(<b>calc(1turn - 32deg)</b>); /* radian calculations, calc within other CSS functions */</div><div>   background: hsl(180, <b>calc(2*25%), 65%</b>); /* calc color values. Read: relative colors */</div><div>   line-height: <b>calc(8/3);</b> /* don't have to do the math */</div><div>   width: <b>calc(23vmin - 2*3rem)</b>;} /* don't understand this one */</div><div><br/></div><div><span style="font-size: 17px;"><b>Object-Fit &amp; Object-Position Properties</b></span></div><div><i><b>img.object-fit</b></i> {</div><div>object-fit: fill | contain | cover | none | scale-down; /* fill: stretch to fill. contain: letterbox. cover: constrain and fill. * /</div><div>object-position: 50% 50%; /* default value: image is centered*/</div><div>object-position: 0 0; /* positioned top left of the content box */<br/></div><div>}</div><div><br/></div><div><b>Chrome = 60% Browser Market Share as of 12/16</b></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><hr/><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none;
