font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; clear: both;"><div><span style="font-size: 17px;"><b>Flexbox Primer</b></span></div><div><i><b><br/></b></i></div><div><b><i>.container</i></b>  {</div><div style="margin-left:40px;"><i>display</i>: flex; /* or inline-flex */</div><div style="margin-left:40px;"><i>flex-direction</i>: row | row-reverse | column | column-reverse;</div><div style="margin-left:40px;"><i>flex-wrap</i>: nowrap | wrap | wrap-reverse;</div><div style="margin-left:40px;"><i>flex-flow</i>: &lt;‘flex-direction’&gt; || &lt;‘flex-wrap’&gt;</div><div style="margin-left:40px;"><i>justify-content</i>: flex-start | flex-end | center | space-between | space-around;</div><div style="margin-left:40px;"><i>align-items</i>: flex-start | flex-end | center | baseline | stretch;</div><div style="margin-left:40px;"><i>align-content</i>: flex-start | flex-end | center | space-between | space-around | stretch;</div><div>}</div><div><br/></div><div><b><i>.item  </i></b>{</div><div style="margin-left:40px;"><i>order</i>: &lt;integer&gt;;</div><div style="margin-left:40px;"><i>flex-grow</i>: &lt;number&gt;; /* default 0 */</div><div style="margin-left:40px;"><i>flex-shrink</i>: &lt;number&gt;; /* default 1 */</div><div style="margin-left:40px;"><i>flex-basis</i>: &lt;length&gt; | auto; /* default auto */</div><div style="margin-left:40px;"><i>flex</i>: none | [ &lt;'flex-grow'&gt; &lt;'flex-shrink'&gt;? || &lt;'flex-basis'&gt; ];</div><div style="margin-left:40px;"><i>align-self</i>: auto | flex-start | flex-end | center | baseline | stretch;</div><div>}</div><div><br/></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><hr/><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0px 0px 0.7em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: 300; font-stretch: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0px 0px 0.7em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: 300; font-stretch: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0px 0px 5px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; width: 660px; word-wrap: break-word; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; clear: both;"><div><br/></div><div><b>em</b></div><div>The em unit can be used to declare font-sizes. In fact, it’s a best practice to use relative units like em for font-size.<br/></div><div><b><br/></b></div><div><b>rem</b></div><div>means Root EM. It’s built to provide some relief the em computational problem that many faced.</div><div>It is a unit of typography equal to the root font-size defined in &lt;html&gt;.</div><div><br/></div><div><b>box-sizing</b>: content-box|border-box|initial|inherit;</div><div><br/></div><div><b>Transition Timing Function in CSS</b></div><div>transition-timing-function: ease | ease-in | ease-out |ease-in-out | linear | step-start | step-end | steps(4, end) | cubic-bezier(0.1, 0.7, 1.0, 0.1);</div><div><br/></div><div><b>CSS3 2016 Quick Updates</b></div><ul><li>apply pseudo-elements on so style broken images</li><li>contain: strict reduces painting costs</li><li>fluid type with font-size: calc (1em + 1vw)</li><li>nested links with &lt;object&gt;</li><li>consider critical progressive CSS (HTTP/2)</li><li>use native variables with CSS currentColor</li><li>service workers can boost performance a lot</li><li>test scan levels to improve image delivery</li><li>early fetch of critical resources with preload</li><li>use the Font Loading API to load web fonts</li><li>replace age prompt with a year prompt</li><li>replace country selector with autosuggest<br/><br/></li></ul></div></div></div></div></div></div><hr/><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0px 0px 0.7em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: 300; font-stretch: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0px 0px 0.7em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: 300; font-stretch: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0px 0px 5px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; width: 660px; word-wrap: break-word; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; clear: both;"><div><span style="font-size: 23px;"><b>2016 New Terminology</b></span></div><div><b> </b></div><div><b>BEM — Block___Element__Modifier</b></div><div>is a methodology (READ: NAMING CONVENTION IN CSS) that helps you to create reusable components and code sharing in front-end development</div><div style="margin-right: -16px; padding-left: 16px; padding-right: 16px; overflow: hidden; transition: max-height 0.3s; max-height: 0px; color: rgb(34, 34, 34); font-family: Roboto, arial, sans-serif; font-size: small; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);margin-left:0px;"><div><br/></div></div><div><b><br/></b></div><div><b>Transclusion</b></div><div>In computer science, transclusion is the inclusion of a document or part of a document into another document by reference. So in the context of Angular, transclusion would be the embedding of an end user template into the directive template, or the directive template into the end user template.<br/></div><div><b><br/></b></div><div><b>Service Workers</b></div><div>Rich offline experiences, periodic background syncs, push notifications—functionality that would normally require a native application—are coming to the web. Service workers provide the technical foundation that all these features rely on.</div><div><br/></div><div>Service workers essentially act as proxy servers that sit between web applications, and the browser and network (when available). They are intended to (amongst other things) enable the creation of effective offline experiences, intercepting network requests and taking appropriate action based on whether the network is available and updated assets reside on the server. They will also allow access to push notifications and background sync APIs.<br/></div><div><br/></div><div><b>MVW (Model-View-Whatever)</b></div><div>paradigm is a term used to indicate the capability of the framework being used to give the option to choose from MVC or MVVM approaches. Like in Angular.js. The Angular team wants you to use “whatever” of the following systems work for you. you can use Model View Controller, Model View Adapter, Model-View-ViewModel etc</div><div><br/></div><div><b>Composability</b></div><div>is a system design principle that deals with the inter-relationships of components. A highly composable system provides recombinant components that can be selected and assembled in various combinations to satisfy specific user requirements.</div><div><br/></div><div><b>Mid·dle·ware</b></div><div>software that acts as a bridge between an operating system or database and applications, especially on a network.</div><div><br/></div><div><b>Data binding</b></div><div>is the process that establishes a connection between the application UI and business logic. If the bindinghas the correct settings and the data provides the proper notifications, then, when the data changes its value, the elements that are bound to the data reflect changes automatically.</div><div><br/></div><div><b>Webpack</b></div><div>is a popular module bundler, a tool for bundling application source code in convenient chunks and for loading that code from a server into a browser.</div><div><br/></div><div><b>Compiling</b></div><div>is the general term for taking source code written in one language and transforming into another.</div><div><br/></div><div><b>Transpiling</b></div><div>is a specific term for taking source code written in one language and transforming into another language that has a similar level of abstraction.</div><div><br/></div><div><b>microservices</b></div><div>are small, independent processes that communicate with each other to form complex applications which utilize language-agnostic APIs. These services are small building blocks, highly decoupled and focused on doing a small task, facilitating a modular approach to system-building.</div><div><br/></div><div><b>A service-oriented architecture (SOA)</b></div><div>is a design pattern in which application components provide services to other components via a communications protocol, typically over a network. The principles of service-orientation are independent of any vendor, product or technology.</div><div><br/></div><div><b>A software system is called &quot;monolithic&quot;</b></div><div>if it has a monolithic architecture, in which functionally distinguishable aspects (for example data input and output, data processing, error handling, and the user interface), are not architecturally separate components but are all interwoven.</div><div><br/></div><div><b>JSX</b></div><div>is a preprocessor step that adds XML syntax to JavaScript. You can definitely use React without JSX but JSX makes React a lot more elegant. Just like XML, JSXtags have a tag name, attributes, and children. If an attribute value is enclosed in quotes, that value is a string.</div><div><br/></div><div><b>PostCSS</b></div><div>aims to reinvent CSS with an ecosystem of custom plugins and tools. Working with the same principles of preprocessors such as Sass and LESS, it transforms extended syntaxes and features into modern, browser-friendly CSS. <i>How you ask? JavaScript.</i></div><div><b><br/></b></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><hr/><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0px 0px 0.7em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: 300; font-stretch: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0px 0px 0.7em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: 300; font-stretch: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0px 0px 5px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; width: 660px; word-wrap: break-word; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; clear: both;"><div><b>Architectural Styles for APIs: REST (also HATEOAS) and RPC (SOAP and JSON-RPC)</b></div><div>In general, When you're publishing an API to the outside world that is either complex or likely to change, SOAP will be more useful. Other than that, REST is usually the better option.</div><div><b><br/></b></div><div><b>REST Style</b></div><div>REST (Representational State Transfer) is an architectural style for services, and as such it defines a set of architectural constraints and agreements. A service, which complies with the REST constraints, is said to be RESTful.</div><div><b><br/></b></div><div><b>HATEOAS Style</b></div><div>HATEOAS is an abbreviation for Hypermedia As The Engine Of Application State. HATEOAS is an extension of REST and any of the constraints and advantages of REST also apply to HATEOAS.</div><div><b><br/></b></div><div><b>RPC is an abbreviation for Remote Procedure Call</b></div><div>RPC is an architectural style for distributed systems. It has been around since the 1980s. Today the most widely used RPC styles are <i>JSON-RPC</i> and <i>XML-RPC</i>. Even SOAP can be considered to follow an RPC architectural style.</div><div><br/></div><div><b>SOAP Style</b></div><div>SOAP follows the RPC style and exposes procedures as central concepts (e.g. getCustomer).</div><div><br/></div><div><i><br/></i></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><hr/><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; style="font-size: 17px;">(Stripe, PayPal, Braintree)</span><ul><li><b>SUBCATEGORIES:</b> Payment Tools, Payment Services, <b>Saas for Stripe</b>, <b>Payments Analytics</b>, <b>Bitcoin Services</b></li></ul></li><li><b><span style="font-size: 17px;">Analytics </span></b><span style="font-size: 17px;">(Google Analytics, Mixpanel, Optimizely)</span><ul><li><b>SUBCATEGORIES:</b> <b>Funnel Analysis Analytics</b>, Predictive Analytics, Custom Analytics, Monitoring for Analytics, Heatmap Analytics, <b>Realtime Analytics</b>, A/B Testing Analytics, General Analytics, <b>Analytics Integrator</b>, Video Marketing and Analytics, Mobile Analytics, Customer Analytics, <b>Customer Satisfaction Analytics</b>, <b>Targeted Messaging Analytics Business Dashboards</b>, Business Intelligence</li></ul></li></ul></li><li><span style="font-size: 20px;"><b>DevOps</b></span><ul><li><span style="font-size: 17px;"><b>Build, Test, Deploy </b></span><span style="font-size: 17px;">(GitHub, Git, Docker, NPM, Sublime, BitBucket, Jenkins, Gulp, Bower, Atom, Travis CI, Vim, Ansible, Vagrant)</span><ul><li><b>SUBCATEGORIES:</b> Collaborative Text Editor, <b>Dependency Monitoring</b>, Javascript Optimizers, Python Build Tools, <b>Architecture Design Tools</b>, <b>Package Managers</b>, Integrated Development Environment Tools, Virtual Machine Platforms &amp; Containers, AWS Tools, API Documentation Browser, <b>Microservices Tools</b>, Sandbox as a Service, Browser Testing, Code Collaboration &amp; Version Control, <b>Open Source Service Discovery</b>, Open Source Cloud, Server Configuration and Automation, <b>Code Coverage</b>, <b>Docker Registry</b>, Virtual Machine Management, Continuous Deployment, Javascript Testing Framework, Cloud Management, Virtualization Platform, Server Software, Containers as a Service, Continuous Integration, <b>Hosted Package Repository</b>, Text Editor, Code Review, Virtual Machine, Markdown Editors, <b>Rails Testing Cluster Management</b>, In-Browser Testing, Web Cache, Container Tools, Tools for GitHub, <b>Front End Package Manager</b>, Git Tools, Front End Scaffolding Tools, Mobile Continuous Integration, <b>localhost Tools</b>, <b>Deployment as a Service</b>, Tools for Text Editors, <b>Infrastructure Build Tools, JS Build Tools / JS Task Runners</b>, Beta Testing/Mobile App Distribution, Version Control System, <b>C/C++ Build Tools</b>, <b>Composable Web Service Framework, Fault Tolerance Tools</b>, Live Reloading, <b>Programming &amp; Code Analytics</b>, Go Testing, <b>Database Cluster Management, HTTP Traffic Replay</b>, Website Performance Testing, Test Management, <b>JavaScript Compilers</b>, <b>Code Search</b>, Source Code Management Desktop Apps, <b>Secrets Management, Load Balancer / Reverse Proxy</b>, <b>Headless Browsers</b>, Testing Frameworks</li></ul></li><li><b><span style="font-size: 17px;">Monitoring </span></b><span style="font-size: 17px;">(New Relic, Pingdom, Sentry, Rollbar)</span><ul><li><b>SUBCATEGORIES:</b> Logging Tools, Performance Monitoring, Monitoring Tools, Cloud Monitoring, <b>Event Monitoring</b>, <b>node.js Application Monitoring</b>, <b>Exception Monitoring</b>, Website Monitoring, <b>Monitoring Aggregation</b>, Mobile Error Monitoring, <b>Status Page Hosting</b>, <b>Log Management</b>, Network Monitoring, Front-end Performance Monitoring, Remote Server Task Execution</li></ul></li></ul></li><li><span style="font-size: 20px;"><b>Business Tools</b></span><ul><li><span style="font-size: 17px;"><b>Collaboration </b></span><span style="font-size: 17px;">(Google Apps, Slack, Trello, Jira, Skype, Asana, Hipchat, Basalmiq, Pivotal)</span><ul><li><b>SUBCATEGORIES:</b> Meeting Tools, Slack Tools, Issue Tracking, Wireframing, Document Signature, Screen Sharing, Team Task Management, Visual Collaboration, Agile Project Management, Time Tracking, Password Management, Group Chat &amp; Notifications, <b>Enterprise Collaboration</b>, Document Collaboration, <b>Hosted IRC</b>, Writing Collaboration, Virtual Desktop, Productivity Suite, <b>Visual Version Control</b>, Kanban for GitHub Issues, Project Management, Web and Video Conferencing, Team Inbox, Meeting Scheduling, <b>ChatOps</b>, <b>Device Streaming</b></li></ul></li><li><b><span style="font-size: 17px;">Back Office </span></b><span style="font-size: 17px;">(GSheets, Xero, NetSuite ERP, Gusto Payroll, Zenefits, AnyPerk)</span><ul><li><b>SUBCATEGORIES:</b> Employee Perks, Fax, Accounting, Payroll &amp; Benefits, <b>Enterprise Resource Planning (ERP), Expense Management</b>, <b>Compliance</b>, Spreadsheets Online, Legal Services</li></ul></li><li><b><span style="font-size: 17px;">Support, Sales, and Marketing </span></b><span style="font-size: 17px;">(Wordpress, MailChimp, ZenDesk, Intercom, AdRoll, HubSpot, Drupal, Marketo, Salesforce)</span><ul><li><b>SUBCATEGORIES:</b> Forums, Online Email Editor, <b>Call Center as a Service</b>, <b>Mail Merge Tools</b>, Self-Hosted Blogging/CMS, CMS Tools, <b>Social Proof Widget</b>, Email Testing, Social Media Tools, Customer Support Chat, Crowdfunding, <b>Competitions as a Service</b>, Marketing Automation, Bug Reporting, <b>Ad Retargeting</b>, Customer Community, <b>Invitation Management</b>, Feedback Widget, Mobile Customer Support, Survey Widget, <b>Cloud Content Management System</b>, Email Marketing, Customer Profiles, Hosted Blogging Platforms, CRM, Help Desk, Landing Pages, <b>SEO as a Service</b>, <b>Web Service Automation</b>, Engagement/Lifecycle Marketing</li></ul></li><li><b><span style="font-size: 17px;">Design </span></b><span style="font-size: 17px;">(InVision)</span><ul><li><b>SUBCATEGORIES:</b> Interactive Mockups, Open Source Design Tools</li></ul></li></ul></li></ul><div><b><br/></b></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><hr/><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0px 0px 0.7em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: 300; font-stretch: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0px 0px 0.7em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: 300; font-stretch: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0px 0px 5px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; width: 660px; word-wrap: break-word; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; clear: both;"><div><span style="font-size: 20px;"><b>Design Patterns 2016</b></span></div><div><b><br/></b></div><div><b>Bots become standard UX</b></div><div>If you sign up for a new Slack account, a so-called Slackbot welcomes and on-boards you. The Slackbot not only asks you for your name (which is then automatically saved in your slack account) but for some other things as well.</div><div><b><br/></b></div><div><b>Containers will become huge</b></div><div>Containers have been around for quite some time. But the web development world saw a lot of actions and changes after the introduction of Docker.</div><div><b><img src="_Programming Memorized  2017_files/web-development-trends-2016-docker.jpg" type="image/jpeg" style="height: auto;"/><br/></b></div><div><b>Browser based IDEs</b></div><div>Odds are that you have your own favorite development environment. Maybe you fell in love with VIM years ago or you’re an IntelliJ fanatic. That’s going to change soon as more and more people are starting to use cloud-based versions of IDEs.</div><div><br/></div><div><b>Internet of Things (IoT) will have a huge impact</b></div><div>The Internet of Things has taken app development to a new level. According to Technavio, IoT will grow by 31.72% (CAGR) between 2015 and 2019.</div><div><b><br/></b></div><div><b>Motion User Interface or Motion UI</b></div><div>Motion UI is a Sass library which is one of the three parts of Foundation for Apps by Zurb.</div><div><br/></div><div><b>Foundation for Apps</b></div><div>Foundation for Apps is an upcoming single page app framework which is built around AngularJS and the flexbox grid framework. This framework enables quick and easy responsive web app creation facilitating developers to quickly start writing code that’s unique to the application.</div><div><b><br/></b></div><div><b>Long Scrolling</b></div><div>Sites with long or infinite scrolling are a quickly cementing themselves as a web design staple.</div><div><br/></div><div><b>More Vibrant Colors</b></div><div>All throughout 2015 we saw the trend of bright colors, and in 2016 we’re seeing them taken to the next level. Expect even more vibrant colors — and more of them in larger palettes.</div><div><br/></div><div><b>HD Visuals</b></div><div>With high-resolution devices quickly becoming the standard, 2016 is quickly becoming the year of HD design. Enthralling videos, powerful photography, and rich graphics are all part of the movement towards HD visuals.</div><div><b><br/></b></div><div><b>Dramatic Typography</b></div><div>Better device resolutions, faster internet speeds, and the availability of new web type tools (Google Fonts, Adobe Typekit, etc.) make this the golden age of typography.</div><div><br/></div><div><i>Popular sans serif fonts:</i></div><div>- Proxima Nova, Futura, Avenir, Open Sans, Helvetica Neue</div><div><br/></div><div><i>Popular serif fonts:</i></div><div>- Caslon, Garamond, Freight Text, Minion, FF Meta Serif</div><div><b><br/></b></div><div><b>Rich animations</b></div><div>Animation ranges in scale, from a tiny, intricate spinners to a full-blown, lively illustration in the foreground or background.</div><div><b><br/></b></div><div><b>Material design</b></div><div>is Google’s simple layered design language. Flat design is a simple alternative to skeuomorphism developed to facilitate early mobile devices.  Generally known as Flat Design 2.0, the hybrid style reflects the modern aesthetic of flat design and the layered feel of Material Design.<br/></div><div><b><br/></b></div><div><b>Microinteractions</b></div><div>Crucial for mobile app design, microinteractions are the minor interactions between bigger interactions, often small enough that users engage them without a second thought.</div><div><br/></div><div>Tapping an alarm to turn it off, a button color change to indicate it’s been pressed, a “ding” indicating a new comment on your picture — microinteractions all add up for a more fulfilling user experience overall.</div><div><br/></div><div><b>Cards</b></div><div>We’ve known the efficiency of cards long before digital design (think business cards, playing cards, etc.). The idea is that all the most relevant information about a single topic is organized into a single container.</div><div><br/></div><div>First championed by social sites like Pinterest, Facebook, and Twitter, today the influence of cards is spreading out across multiple industries.</div><div><br/></div><div><b>Progressive Content Density</b></div><div>In more vertical layouts, keep the top or first screens minimal with ample negative space, and then increase the content density as the scroll deepens.</div><div><b><br/></b></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><hr/><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0px 0px 0.7em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: 300; font-stretch: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0px 0px 0.7em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: 300; font-stretch: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0px 0px 5px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; width: 660px; word-wrap: break-word; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; clear: both;"><div><span style="font-size: 20px;"><b>2016 Jargon/Terminology Update/Refresher</b></span></div><div><b><br/></b></div><div><b>Cookie:</b></div><div>A cookie is a message given to a web browser (the application you use to get online) by a web server. Cookies help identify website users who have visited previously, or those that are there for the first time, and can prepare customized content for them depending on those criteria.</div><div><br/></div><div><b>301 redirect</b></div><div> A permanent redirect from one URL to another, usually from your old website to the new website. 301 redirects are also used to redirect traffic from old web pages to the new pages that have taken their place. (e.g.  “<a dir="ltr" href="http://website.com/about-us">website.com/about-us</a>” is now “<a dir="ltr" href="http://website.com/our-company">website.com/our-company</a>” on the new website.</div><div><br/></div><div><b>Skeuomorphism:</b></div><div>Complicated word, but definitely an important one. Skeuomorphism is almost the opposite of flat design. Remember Apple’s old iOS design that was filled with apps and graphics that looked like they were taken from real life (the compass, the newsstand, the calendar…)?</div><div><br/></div><div><b>Metro Design</b>:</div><div>Also known as “Microsoft Design Language”, this design method was developed by Microsoft and is today used on many of the company’s products. It was inspired by public transportation signs and it aspires to reach the same kind of visual clarity.<br/></div><div><br/></div><div><b>.HTACCESS </b></div><div>The .htaccess file is the default directory-level configuration file on Apache servers. They are also known as “distributed configuration files.” Configuration directives contained in the .htaccess file apply to the directory in which the file is placed as well as all of its subdirectories. Within the .htaccess file things like authorization and authentication, rewriting of URLs, cache control and customized error responses can all be specified.</div><div><br/></div><div><b>BACKLINK </b></div><div>Backlinks are links from other sites back to your own. They’re sometimes also referred to as “trackbacks” (especially on blogs).</div><div><br/></div><div><b>CLIENT-SIDE </b></div><div>Client-side refers to scripts that are run in a viewer’s browser, instead of on a web server (as in server-side scripts).</div><div><br/></div><div><b>SERVER-SIDE </b></div><div>Server-side refers to scripts run on a web server, as opposed to in a user’s browser. Server-side scripts often take a bit longer to run than a client-side script, as each page must reload when an action is taken.</div><div><br/></div><div><b>DNS </b></div><div>Stands for Domain Name Service (alternately Domain Name System or Domain Name Server). Basically, it’s the thing that converts IP addresses into domain names.</div><div><br/></div><div><b>DTD </b></div><div>Stands for Document Type Definition. DTD is one of several SGML and XML schema languages. It provides a list of the attributes, comments, elements, entities, and notes in a document along with their relationships to each other.</div><div><br/></div><div><b>EXTENSIBLE MARKUP LANGUAGE </b></div><div>Otherwise known as XML. XML is a markup language used for writing custom markup languages.</div><div><b><br/></b></div><div><b>AJAX </b></div><div>Stands for Asynchronous JavaScript and XML. AJAX is typically used for creating dynamic web applications and allows for asynchronous data retrieval without having to reload the page a visitor is on.</div><div><br/></div><div><b>SGML</b></div><div>Stands for Standard Generalized Markup Language. It’s a markup language used for defining the structure of a document. SGML isn’t mentioned very often, but it’s the markup language that serves as the basis for both XML and HTML.</div><div><br/></div><div><b>SPECIFICATION </b></div><div>A specification is a document that offers an explicit definition and requirements for a web service or technology and generally includes how the technology is meant to be used, along with the tags, elements, and any dependencies.</div><div><b><br/></b></div><div><b>SCHEMA</b></div><div>Generally, a schema is an XML document used in place of a DTD to describe other XML documents.</div><div>- XML Schema Tutorial from w3schools</div><div><span style="color: rgb(36, 39, 41);"><span style="font-size: 15px;"><span style="font-family: Arial, 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, sans-serif;"><b><br/></b></span></span></span></div><div><span style="color: rgb(36, 39, 41);"><span style="font-size: 15px;"><span style="font-family: Arial, 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, sans-serif;"><b>Shim vs Polyfill</b></span></span></span></div><div><span style="color: rgb(36, 39, 41);"><span style="font-size: 15px;"><span style="font-family: Arial, 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, sans-serif;">A <b>polyfill</b> is a type of shim that retrofits legacy browsers with modern HTML5/CSS3 features.</span></span></span></div><div><span style="color: rgb(36, 39, 41);"><span style="font-size: 15px;"><span style="font-family: Arial, 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, sans-serif;">A <b>shim</b>, on the other hand, performs interception of an API call and provides a layer of abstraction.</span></span></span></div></div></div><div><br/></div></div></div></div></div><hr/><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0px 0px 0.7em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: 300; font-stretch: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0px 0px 0.7em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: 300; font-stretch: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div><span style="font-size: 21px;"><b><span style="font-family: Oxygen;"><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 64);">SQL Refresher</span></span></b></span></div><div><br/></div><div><b>CREATE TABLE</b> creates a new table.</div><div><b>INSERT INTO</b> adds a new row to a table.</div><div><b>UPDATE</b> edits a row in a table</div><div><b>ALTER TABLE</b> changes an existing table.</div><div><br/></div><div><b>SELECT</b> queries data from a table.</div><div><b>WHERE</b> is a popular command that lets you filter the results of the query based on conditions that you specify.</div><div><b>LIKE and BETWEEN</b> are special operators that can be used in a WHERE clause</div><div><b>AND and OR</b> are special operators that you can use with WHERE to filter the query on two or more conditions.</div><div><b>ORDER BY</b> lets you sort the results of the query in either ascending or descending order.</div><div><b>LIMIT</b> lets you specify the maximum number of rows that the query will return. This is especially important in large tables that have thousands or even millions of rows.</div><div><b>DELETE FROM</b> deletes rows from a table.</div><div><br/></div><div><ul style="margin: 0.7em 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-weight: 300; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Oxygen, Oxygen, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; list-style: none; color: rgb(62, 62, 64); letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><li>The <code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;">UNION</code> clause allows us to utilize information from multiple tables in our queries.<br/>
The <code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;">UNION ALL</code> clause allows us to utilize information from multiple tables in our queries, including duplicate values.<br/><code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;">INTERSECT</code> is used to combine two <code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;">SELECT</code> statements, but returns rows only from the first <code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;">SELECT</code> statement that are identical to a row in the second <code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;">SELECT</code> statement.<br/><code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;">EXCEPT</code> returns distinct rows from the first <code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;">SELECT</code> statement that aren’t output by the second <code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;">SELECT</code> statement</li></ul></div><div><br/></div><div><ul style="margin: 0.7em 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-weight: 300; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Oxygen, Oxygen, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; list-style: none; color: rgb(62, 62, 64); letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><li><em style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: italic; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box;"><b>Aggregate functions</b></em> combine multiple rows together to form a single value of more meaningful information.</li><li><code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;"><b>COUNT</b></code><b> </b>takes the name of a column(s) as an argument and counts the number of rows where the value(s) is not <code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;">NULL</code>.</li><li><code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;"><b>GROUP BY</b></code> is a clause used with aggregate functions to combine data from one or more columns.</li><li><code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;"><b>SUM()</b></code> takes the column name as an argument and returns the sum of all the values in that column.</li><li><code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;"><b>MAX()</b></code> takes the column name as an argument and returns the largest value in that column.</li><li><code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;"><b>MIN()</b></code> takes the column name as an argument and returns the smallest value in that column.</li><li><code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;"><b>AVG()</b></code> takes a column name as an argument and returns the average value for that column.</li><li><code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;"><b>ROUND()</b></code><b> </b>takes two arguments, a column name and the number of decimal places to round the values in that column.</li></ul></div><div><ul style="margin: 0.7em 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: 300; font-stretch: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; list-style: none; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><li><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 64);"><em style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: italic; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box;"><b>Primary Key</b></em><span style="font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: Oxygen, Oxygen, 'Segoe UI', 'Helvetica Neue', sans-serif;"> is a column that serves a unique identifier for row in the table. Values in this column must be unique and cannot be </span></span></span><code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;">NULL</code><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 64);"><span style="font-family: Oxygen, Oxygen, 'Segoe UI', 'Helvetica Neue', sans-serif;">.<br/></span><em style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: italic; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box;"><b>Foreign Key</b></em><span style="font-family: Oxygen, Oxygen, 'Segoe UI', 'Helvetica Neue', sans-serif;"> is a column that contains the primary key to another table in the database. It is used to identify a particular row in the referenced table.</span><em style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: italic; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box;">Joins</em><span style="font-family: Oxygen, Oxygen, 'Segoe UI', 'Helvetica Neue', sans-serif;"> are used in SQL to combine data from multiple tables.<br/></span></span><code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;"><b>INNER JOIN</b></code><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 64);"><span style="font-family: Oxygen, Oxygen, 'Segoe UI', 'Helvetica Neue', sans-serif;"> will combine rows from different tables if the </span><em style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: italic; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box;">join condition</em><span style="font-family: Oxygen, Oxygen, 'Segoe UI', 'Helvetica Neue', sans-serif;">is true.<br/></span></span><code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;"><b>LEFT OUTER JOIN</b></code><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 64);"><span style="font-family: Oxygen, Oxygen, 'Segoe UI', 'Helvetica Neue', sans-serif;"> will return every row in the </span><em style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: italic; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box;">left</em><span style="font-family: Oxygen, Oxygen, 'Segoe UI', 'Helvetica Neue', sans-serif;"> table, and if the join condition is not met,<br/></span></span><code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;"><b>NULL</b></code><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 64);"><span style="font-family: Oxygen, Oxygen, 'Segoe UI', 'Helvetica Neue', sans-serif;"> values are used to fill in the columns from the </span><em style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: italic; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box;">right</em><span style="font-family: Oxygen, Oxygen, 'Segoe UI', 'Helvetica Neue', sans-serif;"> table.<br/></span></span><code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;"><b>AS</b></code><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 64);"><span style="font-family: Oxygen, Oxygen, 'Segoe UI', 'Helvetica Neue', sans-serif;"> is a keyword in SQL that allows you to rename a column or table in the result set using an </span><em style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: italic; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box;">alias</em><span style="font-family: Oxygen, Oxygen, 'Segoe UI', 'Helvetica Neue', sans-serif;">.<br/></span></span> <span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 64); font-family: Oxygen, Oxygen, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: 300; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); display: inline !important; float: none;">Each </span><code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-weight: 300; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;">SELECT</code><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 64); font-family: Oxygen, Oxygen, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: 300; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); display: inline !important; float: none;"> statement within the </span><code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-weight: 300; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;"><b>UNION</b></code><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 64); font-family: Oxygen, Oxygen, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: 300; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); display: inline !important; float: none;"> must have the same number of columns with similar data types. The columns in each </span><code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-weight: 300; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;">SELECT</code><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 64); font-family: Oxygen, Oxygen, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: 300; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); display: inline !important; float: none;"> statement must be in the same order.</span></li><li><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 64);">ALL keyword to display duplicates. </span></li></ul></div><div><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 64);"><br/></span></div><div><p style="margin: 0px 0px 0.7em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-weight: 300; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Oxygen, Oxygen, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(62, 62, 64); letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><b>Date Functions:</b></p><ul style="margin: 0.7em 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-weight: 300; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Oxygen, Oxygen, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; list-style: none; color: rgb(62, 62, 64); letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><li><code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;">DATETIME</code>; Returns the date and time of the column specified. This can be modified to return only the date or only the time.<code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;">DATETIME(time1, +X hours, Y minutes, Z days)</code>: Increments the specificed column by a given number of hours, minutes, or days.</li></ul><p style="margin: 0px 0px 0.7em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-weight: 300; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Oxygen, Oxygen, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(62, 62, 64); letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><b>Numeric Functions:</b></p><ul style="margin: 0.7em 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-weight: 300; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Oxygen, Oxygen, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; list-style: none; color: rgb(62, 62, 64); letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><li><code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;">(number1 + number2);</code>: Returns the sum of two numbers, or other mathematical operations, accordingly.<code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;">CAST(number1 AS REAL) / number2;</code>: Returns the result as a real number by casting one of numeric inputs as a real number<code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;">ROUND(number, precision);</code>: Returns the numeric value rounded off to the next value specified.</li></ul><p style="margin: 0px 0px 0.7em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-weight: 300; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Oxygen, Oxygen, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(62, 62, 64); letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><b>String Functions:</b></p><ul style="margin: 0.7em 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-weight: 300; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Oxygen, Oxygen, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; list-style: none; color: rgb(62, 62, 64); letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><li><code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;">'string1' || ' ' || 'string2';</code>: Concatenates string1 and string 2, with a space between.<code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;">REPLACE(string,from_string,to_string)</code>: Returns the string with all occurrences of the string <code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;">from_string</code> replaced by the string <code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;">to_string</code>.</li></ul></div><div><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 64);"><br/></span></div><div><b>------------Table Transformation-------------</b></div><div><b>Subqueries</b></div><div>- <i>Subqueries</i> are used to complete an SQL transformation by nesting one query within another query.</div><div>- A <i>non-correlated subquery</i> is a subquery that can be run independently of the outer query and can be used to complete a multi-step transformation.</div><div>- A <i>correlated subquery</i> is a subquery that cannot be run independently of the outer query. The order of operations in a correlated subquery is as follows:</div><div><b><br/></b></div><div><b>Non-Correlated Subquery</b></div><div style="margin-left:40px;">SELECT id</div><div style="margin-left:40px;">FROM flights AS f</div><div style="margin-left:40px;">WHERE distance &gt; ( SELECT AVG(distance)</div><div style="margin-left:40px;">FROM flights</div><div style="margin-left:40px;">WHERE carrier = f.carrier);<br/></div><div style="margin-left:40px;"><b><br/></b></div><div><b>Correlated Subquery</b></div><div style="margin-left:40px;">SELECT origin, id, (SELECT COUNT(*)</div><div style="margin-left:40px;">    FROM flights AS f</div><div style="margin-left:40px;">    WHERE f.id &lt; flights.id</div><div style="margin-left:40px;">    AND f.origin=flights.origin) + 1</div><div style="margin-left:40px;">    AS flight_sequence_number</div><div style="margin-left:40px;">    FROM flights;</div><div><br/></div><div><b>----------------Combining Table Data--------------------</b></div><div><br/></div><div>There are two ways of doing this:</div><div><b>- Merge the rows, called a join.</b></div><div><b>- Merge the columns, called a union.</b></div><div><b><br/></b></div><div><b>Query Table Union</b></div><div style="margin-left:40px;">SELECT id, avg(a.sale_price) FROM (</div><div style="margin-left:40px;">  SELECT id, sale_price FROM order_items</div><div style="margin-left:40px;">  UNION ALL</div><div style="margin-left:40px;">  SELECT id, sale_price FROM order_items_historic) AS a</div><div style="margin-left:40px;">  GROUP BY 1;</div><div style="margin-left:40px;"><br/></div></div></div></div></div><hr/><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0px 0px 0.7em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: 300; font-stretch: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0px 0px 0.7em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: 300; font-stretch: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div><span style="font-size: 21px;"><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 64);"><span style="font-family: Oxygen;"><b>Git Refresher</b></span></span></span></div><div><b><br/></b></div><div><b>Starting a Repo: </b>init | clone | remote</div><div><b>Showing/Undoing Changes: </b>status | diff | log | blame | reset | revert</div><div><b>Staging: </b>add | rm</div><div><b>Publishing: </b>commit | stash | push</div><div><b>Updating and Getting Code: </b>fetch | pull</div><div><b>Branching: </b>branch | checkout | merge | rebase</div><div><br/></div><ul><li>git branch: Lists all a Git project's branches.</li><li>git branch branch_name: Creates a new branch.</li><li>git checkout branch_name: Used to switch from one branch to another.</li><li>git merge branch_name: Used to join file changes from one branch to another.</li><li>git branch -d branch_name: Deletes the branch specified.</li><li>git commit -m 'some message.</li><li>git clone: Creates a local copy of a remote.</li><li>git remote -v: Lists a Git project's remotes.</li><li>git fetch: Fetches work from the remote into the local copy.</li><li>git merge origin/master: Merges origin/master into your local branch.</li><li>git push origin &lt;branch_name&gt;: Pushes a local branch to the</li><li>origin remote.</li></ul><div><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 64);"><br/></span></div></div></div></div></div><hr/><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div><div style="margin: 0px 0px 0.7em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: 300; font-stretch: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 64);"><span style="font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: Oxygen, Oxygen, 'Segoe UI', 'Helvetica Neue', sans-serif;"><b>Default HTML box model is content-box.</b></span></span></span></div><div><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 64);"><span style="font-family: Oxygen, Oxygen, 'Segoe UI', 'Helvetica Neue', sans-serif;">Fortunately, we can reset the entire box model and specify a new one: </span></span><code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;"><b>border-box</b></code><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 64);"><span style="font-family: Oxygen, Oxygen, 'Segoe UI', 'Helvetica Neue', sans-serif;"><b>.</b></span></span></div></div><pre style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-weight: 300; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(62, 62, 64); letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"></pre><div style="margin: 0px; padding: 1rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: 300; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 13px; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; display: block; height: auto; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); position: relative; overflow: auto; background: rgb(53, 69, 81); text-shadow: rgba(43, 56, 66, 0.298039) 1px 1px 1px; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased;"><code style="margin: 0.7em 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: transparent; white-space: nowrap; display: block;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 15.2px; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; display: block; white-space: pre-wrap;">* { <span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 13px; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(131, 255, 245);">box-sizing</span>: <span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 13px; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(204, 123, 194);">border-box</span>; }</span></code></div><div style="margin: 0px 0px 0.7em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: 300; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Oxygen, Oxygen, 'Segoe UI', 'Helvetica Neue', sans-serif; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(62, 62, 64); letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div><code style="margin: 0.7em 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline;
