word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: transparent; white-space: nowrap; display: block;">The code in the example above resets the box model to <code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;">border-box</code> for all HTML elements.</code></div><div><code style="margin: 0.7em 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: transparent; white-space: nowrap; display: block;"><b>This new box model avoids the dimensional issues that exist in the former box model you learned about.</b></code></div></div></div><div><span style="font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: Oxygen, Oxygen, 'Segoe UI', 'Helvetica Neue', sans-serif;"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 64);"><br/></span></span></span></span></div><div><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 64); font-family: Oxygen, Oxygen, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: 300; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); display: inline !important; float: none;">What's the difference between </span><code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-weight: 300; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;">display: none</code><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 64); font-family: Oxygen, Oxygen, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: 300; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); display: inline !important; float: none;"> and </span><code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-weight: 300; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;">visibility: hidden</code><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 64); font-family: Oxygen, Oxygen, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: 300; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); display: inline !important; float: none;">? An element with </span><code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-weight: 300; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;">display: none</code><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 64); font-family: Oxygen, Oxygen, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: 300; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); display: inline !important; float: none;"> will be completely removed from the web page. An element with </span><code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-weight: 300; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;">visibility: hidden</code><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 64); font-family: Oxygen, Oxygen, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: 300; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); display: inline !important; float: none;">, </span></div><div><span style="font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: Oxygen, Oxygen, 'Segoe UI', 'Helvetica Neue', sans-serif;"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 64);"><br/></span></span></span></span></div></div></div><hr/><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div><span style="font-size: 23px;"><b><span style="font-family: Oxygen, Oxygen, 'Segoe UI', 'Helvetica Neue', sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 64);">Command Line Refresher</span></span></b></span></div><div><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 64);"><strong style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: bold; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Oxygen, Oxygen, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box;">~/.bash_profile</strong><span style="font-family: inherit;"> is where environment settings are stored. You can edit this file with nano.</span></span></div><div><ul style="margin: 0.7em 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: 300; font-stretch: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; list-style: none; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><li style="display:inline;list-style:none;"><ul style="margin: 0.5em 0px 0.7em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; list-style: none;"><li style="display:inline;list-style:none;"><ul style="margin: 0.7em 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: 300; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Oxygen, Oxygen, 'Segoe UI', 'Helvetica Neue', sans-serif; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; list-style: none; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 0.7em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 1em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(62, 62, 64);"><em style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: italic; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box;">environment variables</em> are variables that can be used across commands and programs and hold information about the environment.
<ul style="margin: 0.5em 0px 0.7em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; list-style: none;"><li><code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;">export VARIABLE=&quot;Value&quot;</code><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 64);"> sets and exports an environment variable.<br/></span><code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;">USER</code><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 64);"> is the name of the current user.<br/></span><code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;">PS1</code><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 64);"> is the command prompt.<br/></span><code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;">HOME</code><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 64);"> is the home directory. It is usually not customized.<br/></span><code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;">PATH</code><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 64);"> returns a colon separated list of file paths. It is customized in advanced cases.<br/></span><code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;">env</code><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 64);"> returns a list of environment variables.</span></li></ul></li></ul></li><li><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 64);"><b><span style="font-family: inherit;">redirects standard output of a command to a file, overwriting previous content.<br/></span></b></span><code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;">&gt;&gt;</code><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 64);"><span style="font-family: inherit;"> redirects standard output of a command to a file, appending new content to old content.<br/></span></span><code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;">&lt;</code><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 64);"><span style="font-family: inherit;"> redirects standard input to a command.<br/></span></span><code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;">|</code><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 64);"><span style="font-family: inherit;"> redirects standard output of a command to another command.</span></span></li></ul></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 0.7em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 1em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(62, 62, 64);"><b>A number of other commands are powerful when combined with redirection commands:</b><ul style="margin: 0.5em 0px 0.7em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; list-style: none;"><li><code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;">sort</code><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 64);">: sorts lines of text alphabetically.<br/></span><code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;">uniq</code><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 64);">: filters duplicate, adjacent lines of text.<br/></span><code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;">grep</code><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 64);">: searches for a text pattern and outputs it.<br/></span><code style="margin: 0px 0.0625rem; padding: 0px 0.25rem; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 0.95em; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; border-radius: 0.125rem; color: rgb(32, 64, 86); background-color: rgb(212, 213, 214); white-space: nowrap;">sed</code><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 64);"> : searches for a text pattern, modifies it, and outputs it.</span></li></ul></li><li><b><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 64);">Nano Commands</span></b></li><li><span style="font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 64);">Ctrl + O saves a file. 'O' stands for output.</span></span></li><li><span style="font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 64);">Ctrl + X exits the nano program. 'X' stands for exit.</span></span></li><li><span style="font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 64);">Ctrl + G opens a help menu.</span></span></li><li><span style="font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 64);">clear clears the terminal window, moving the command prompt to the top of the screen.</span></span></li><li><b><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 64);">^ &lt;---THIS MEANS CTRL</span></b></li></ul></div><div><b><br/></b></div></div></div><hr/><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div><b>Sublime Text: Find and Replace Special Characters</b></div><div style="font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; margin-top: 0px !important;"><div><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(34, 34, 34);">Enable regex in the find panel.</span></span></span></div></div><div style="font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px !important;"><div><span style="color: rgb(34, 34, 34);"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;">Then you can use <strong style="font-weight: bold;">\t</strong> for tabs. <strong style="font-weight: bold;">\r</strong> for carriage returns. <strong style="font-weight: bold;">\n</strong> for newlines.</span></span></span></div><div><span style="color: rgb(34, 34, 34);"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;"><br/></span></span></span></div><div><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 64); font-family: Oxygen, Oxygen, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: 300; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); display: inline !important; float: none;">At the time of writing, the <b>W3C recommends 2 spaces of indentation when writing HTML code</b>. Indentation is intended for elements nested within other elements.</span></div><div><span style="color: rgb(34, 34, 34);"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;"><br/></span></span></span></div></div></div></div><hr/><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div><b>Computer Science Courses that Don't Exist, But Should</b></div><div><br/></div><div><i>CSCI 2100: Unlearning Object-Oriented Programming</i></div><div>Discover how to create and use variables that aren't inside of an object hierarchy. Learn about &quot;functions,&quot; which are like methods but more generally useful. Prerequisite: Any course that used the term &quot;abstract base class.&quot;</div><div><br/></div><div><i>CSCI 3300: Classical Software Studies</i></div><div>Discuss and dissect historically significant products, including VisiCalc, AppleWorks, Robot Odyssey, Zork, and MacPaint. Emphases are on user interface and creativity fostered by hardware limitations.</div><div><br/></div><div><i>CSCI 4020: Writing Fast Code in Slow Languages</i></div><div>Analyze performance at a high level, writing interpreted Python that matches or beats typical C++ code while being less fragile and more fun to work with.</div><div><br/></div><div><i>CSCI 2170: User Experience of Command Line Tools</i></div><div>An introduction to UX principles as applied to command line programs designed as class projects. Core focus is on output relevance, readability, and minimization. UNIX &quot;ls&quot; tool is a case study in excessive command line switches.</div><div><br/></div><div><i>PSYC 4410: Obsessions of the Programmer Mind</i></div><div>Identify and understand tangential topics that software developers frequently fixate on: code formatting, taxonomy, type systems, splitting projects into too many files. Includes detailed study of knee-jerk criticism when exposed to unfamiliar systems.</div><div><br/></div></div></div><hr/><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: sans-serif;">In <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Computer_networking" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Computer networking">computer networking</a>, a <b>service set</b></span></span></span></div><div><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: sans-serif;">is a set consisting of all the devices associated with a consumer or enterprise <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/IEEE_802.11" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="IEEE 802.11">IEEE 802.11</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wireless_LAN" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Wireless LAN">wireless local area network</a> (WLAN). The service set can be local, independent, extended or mesh.</span></span></span></div></div><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: sans-serif;">Service sets have an associated identifier, the <b>Service Set Identifier (SSID)</b>, which consists of 32 octets that frequently contains a human readable identifier of the network.</span></span></span></div><div><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: sans-serif;"><br/></span></span></span></div><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; color: rgb(37, 37, 37); font-family: sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div>A <b>wireless local area network</b> (<b>WLAN</b>)</div><div>is a <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wireless_network" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Wireless network">wireless computer network</a> that links two or more devices using a wireless distribution method (often <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spread_spectrum" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Spread spectrum">spread-spectrum</a> or <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OFDM" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="OFDM">OFDM</a> radio) within a <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/LAN" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="LAN">limited area</a> such as a home, school, computer laboratory, or office building. This gives users the ability to move around within a local coverage area and yet still be connected to the network. A WLAN can also provide a connection to the wider <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Internet" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Internet">Internet</a>.</div></div><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: sans-serif;">Most modern WLANs are based on <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/IEEE_802.11" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="IEEE 802.11">IEEE 802.11</a> standards and are marketed under the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wi-Fi" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Wi-Fi">Wi-Fi</a> brand name.</span></span></span></div><div><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: sans-serif;"><br/></span></span></span></div><div><p style="margin: 0.5em 0px; color: rgb(37, 37, 37); font-family: sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><b>IEEE 802.11</b> is a set of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Media_access_control" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Media access control">media access control</a> (MAC) and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Physical_layer" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Physical layer">physical layer</a> (PHY) specifications for implementing <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wireless_LAN" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Wireless LAN">wireless local area network</a> (WLAN) computer communication in the 900 MHz and 2.4, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/IEEE_802.11y-2008" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="IEEE 802.11y-2008">3.6</a>, 5, and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/IEEE_802.11ad" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="IEEE 802.11ad">60 GHz</a> frequency bands. They are created and maintained by the<b> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Institute_of_Electrical_and_Electronics_Engineers" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Institute of Electrical and Electronics Engineers">Institute of Electrical and Electronics Engineers</a> (IEEE)</b> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Local_area_network" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Local area network">LAN</a>/<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Metropolitan_area_network" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Metropolitan area network">MAN</a> Standards Committee (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/IEEE_802" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="IEEE 802">IEEE 802</a>). The base version of the standard was released in 1997, and has had subsequent amendments. The standard and amendments provide the basis for wireless network products using the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wi-Fi" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Wi-Fi">Wi-Fi</a> brand. While each amendment is officially revoked when it is incorporated in the latest version of the standard, the corporate world tends to market to the revisions because they concisely denote capabilities of their products. As a result, in the market place, each revision tends to become its own standard.</p><p style="margin: 0.5em 0px; color: rgb(37, 37, 37); font-family: sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"></p></div><div><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: sans-serif;"><b><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"><br/></span></b></span></span></div></div></div><div><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"><b>Universal Plug and Play</b> (<b>UPnP</b>)</span></span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);">is a set of </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Networking_protocol" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Networking protocol">networking protocols</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"> that permits networked </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Peripheral_device" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Peripheral device">devices</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);">, such as personal computers, printers, Internet gateways, </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wi-Fi" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Wi-Fi">Wi-Fi</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"> access points and mobile devices to seamlessly discover each other's presence on the network and establish functional </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Network_service" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Network service">network services</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"> for data sharing, communications, and entertainment. UPnP is intended primarily for residential networks without enterprise-class devices.</span></span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"><b><br/></b></span></span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"><b>Network address translation</b> (<b>NAT</b>)</span></span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);">is a method of remapping one IP </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Address_space" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Address space">address space</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"> into another by modifying </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Network_address" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Network address">network address</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"> information in </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Internet_Protocol" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Internet Protocol">Internet Protocol</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"> (IP) </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Datagram" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Datagram">datagram</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"> packet headers while they are in transit across a traffic </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Router_(computing)" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Router (computing)">routing device</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);">.<sup style="unicode-bidi: isolate; white-space: nowrap; font-size: 11.2px; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal;"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Network_address_translation#cite_note-1" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none; white-space: nowrap;">[1]</a></sup> The technique was originally used for ease of rerouting traffic in IP networks without readdressing every host. It has become a popular and essential tool in conserving global address space allocations in face of </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/IPv4_address_exhaustion" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="IPv4 address exhaustion">IPv4 address exhaustion</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"> by sharing one Internet-routable IP address of a NAT gateway for an entire private network.</span></span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: sans-serif;"><b><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"><br/></span></b></span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"><b>Network address translator traversal</b></span></span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);">is a computer networking technique of establishing and maintaining </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Internet_protocol" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Internet protocol">Internet protocol</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"> connections across gateways that implement </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Network_address_translation" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Network address translation">network address translation</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"> (NAT). NAT breaks the principle of </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/End-to-end_connectivity" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="End-to-end connectivity">end-to-end connectivity</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);">originally envisioned in the design of the </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Internet" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Internet">Internet</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);">.</span></span></span></div></div><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);">NAT traversal techniques are required for many network applications, such as </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Peer-to-peer" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Peer-to-peer">peer-to-peer</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"> file sharing and </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Voice_over_IP" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Voice over IP">Voice over IP</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);">.<sup style="unicode-bidi: isolate; white-space: nowrap; font-size: 11.2px; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal;"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/NAT_traversal#cite_note-ntexpl-1" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none; white-space: nowrap;">[1]</a></sup></span></span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"><b><br/></b></span></span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"><b>Internet Gateway Device</b> (<b>IGD</b>) <b>Standardized Device Control Protocol</b><sup style="font-size: 11.2px; white-space: nowrap;">[<i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (April 2016)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup></span></span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);">is a protocol for mapping </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Port_(computer_networking)" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Port (computer networking)">ports</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"> in </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Network_address_translation" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Network address translation">network address translation</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"> (NAT) setups, supported by a certain number of NAT-enabled </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Router_(computing)" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Router (computing)">routers</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);">.<sup style="unicode-bidi: isolate; white-space: nowrap; font-size: 11.2px; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal;"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Internet_Gateway_Device_Protocol#cite_note-1" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none; white-space: nowrap;">[1]</a></sup> It is a common </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Communications_protocol" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Communications protocol">communications protocol</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"> of automatically configuring </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Port_forwarding" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Port forwarding">port forwarding</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);">, and is part of an </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/International_Organization_for_Standardization" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="International Organization for Standardization">ISO</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);">/</span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/International_Electrotechnical_Commission" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="International Electrotechnical Commission">IEC</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"> Standard <sup style="unicode-bidi: isolate; white-space: nowrap; font-size: 11.2px; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal;"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Internet_Gateway_Device_Protocol#cite_note-ISO.2FIEC_29341-2" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none; white-space: nowrap;">[2]</a></sup> rather than an </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Internet_Engineering_Task_Force" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Internet Engineering Task Force">Internet Engineering Task Force</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"> standard.</span></span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"><br/></span></span></span></div><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);">In </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Computer_networking" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Computer networking">computer networking</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);">, <b>port forwarding</b> or <b>port mapping</b></span></span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);">is an application of </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Network_address_translation" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Network address translation">network address translation</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"> (NAT) that redirects a communication request from one </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/IP_address" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="IP address">address</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"> and </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Port_number" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Port number">port number</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"> combination to another while the </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Network_packet" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Network packet">packets</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"> are traversing a network gateway, such as a </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Router_(computing)" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Router (computing)">router</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"> or </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Firewall_(computing)" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Firewall (computing)">firewall</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);">. This technique is most commonly used to make services on a host residing on a protected or </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/IP_masquerading" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="IP masquerading">masqueraded</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"> (internal) network available to hosts on the opposite side of the gateway (external network), by remapping the destination IP address and port number of the communication to an internal host.<sup style="unicode-bidi: isolate; white-space: nowrap; font-size: 11.2px; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal;"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Port_forwarding#cite_note-1" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none; white-space: nowrap;">[1]</a></sup><sup style="unicode-bidi: isolate; white-space: nowrap; font-size: 11.2px; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal;"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Port_forwarding#cite_note-2" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none; white-space: nowrap;">[2]</a></sup></span></span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"><br/></span></span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);">In the field of </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Computer_security" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Computer security">computer security</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);">, <b>command and control</b> (<b>C&amp;C) infrastructure</b></span></span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);">consists of </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Server_(computing)" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Server (computing)">servers</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"> and other technical infrastructure used to control </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Malware" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Malware">malware</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"> in general, and, in particular, </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Botnet" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Botnet">botnets</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);">. <sup style="unicode-bidi: isolate; white-space: nowrap; font-size: 11.2px; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal;"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Command_and_control_(malware)#cite_note-1" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none; white-space: nowrap;">[1]</a></sup><sup style="unicode-bidi: isolate; white-space: nowrap; font-size: 11.2px; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal;"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Command_and_control_(malware)#cite_note-2" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none; white-space: nowrap;">[2]</a></sup> Command and control servers may be either directly controlled by the malware operators, or themselves run on hardware compromised by malware. </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fast-flux_DNS" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Fast-flux DNS">Fast-flux DNS</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"> can be used as a way to make it difficult to track down the control servers, which may change from day to day. Control servers may also hop from DNS domain to DNS domain, with </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Domain_generation_algorithm" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Domain generation algorithm">domain generation algorithms</a></span></span><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"><span style="font-family: sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"> being used to create new DNS names for controller servers.</span><sup style="unicode-bidi: isolate; white-space: nowrap; font-size: 11.2px; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal;"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Command_and_control_(malware)#cite_note-3" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none; white-space: nowrap;">[3</a></sup></span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 11.2px;"><span style="font-family: sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"><sup><br/></sup></span></span></span></div><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"><b>Fast flux</b></span></span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);">is a </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Domain_name_system" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Domain name system">DNS</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"> technique used by </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Botnet" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Botnet">botnets</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"> to hide </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Phishing" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Phishing">phishing</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"> and </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Malware" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Malware">malware</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"> delivery sites behind an ever-changing network of compromised hosts acting as proxies. It can also refer to the combination of </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Peer-to-peer_networking" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Peer-to-peer networking">peer-to-peer networking</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);">, distributed command and control, web-based </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Load_balancing_(computing)" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Load balancing (computing)">load balancing</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"> and </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proxy_server" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Proxy server">proxy</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"> redirection used to make malware networks more resistant to discovery and counter-measures. The </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Storm_Worm" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Storm Worm">Storm Worm</a></span></span><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"><span style="font-family: sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"> (2007) is one of the first malware variants to make use of this technique.</span></span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"><br/></span></span></span></div><div style="margin: 0.5em 0px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"><b>Domain generation algorithms</b></span></span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);">(DGA) are algorithms seen in various families of </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Malware" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Malware">malware</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"> that are used to periodically generate a large number of </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Domain_Name_System" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Domain Name System">domain names</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"> that can be used as rendezvous points with their </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Command_and_control_(malware)" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Command and control (malware)">command and control servers</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);">. The large number of potential rendezvous points makes it difficult for law enforcement to effectively shut down </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Botnet" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Botnet">botnets</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);">, since infected computers will attempt to contact some of these domain names every day to receive updates or commands. By using </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Public-key_cryptography" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Public-key cryptography">public-key cryptography</a><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);">, it is unfeasible for law enforcement and other actors to mimic commands from the malware controllers as some worms will automatically reject any updates not </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Digital_signature" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background: none;" title="Digital signature">signed</a></span></span><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"><span style="font-family: sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"> by the malware controllers.</span></span></span></div><div><span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: sans-serif;"><span style="color: rgb(37, 37, 37);"><br/></span></span></span></div><div><b>Mr. Robot Pringles Cantenna</b></div><div>A slightly less urgent question: What the hell is Eliot doing with that Pringles can?</div><div>He’s building a cantenna! The circuit board he drops inside the can is a wireless card, connected to the computer through USB. The foil in the Pringles can blocks out radio signal, so the antenna can only pick up on signals coming directly down the tube. That lets him connect to wireless signals much farther away, blocking out the extraneous noise that would otherwise drown out weaker signals. Once the tube is pointed at a Wi-Fi network across the street, that’s the only network the antenna can pick up on. Every signal that’s not headed straight down the barrel of the tube gets blocked out. It’s the same trick we saw Darlene pull when they planted the femtocell back in episode five, although she used the shiny, out-of-the-box version that looks like a telescope. This is the hackier version that just looks like, well, a Pringles can.</div></div></div></div></div><div><b><br/></b></div><hr/><div><b>AngularJS</b></div><div><b><br/></b></div><div><p style="margin: 0px 0px 0.7em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-weight: 300; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Oxygen, Oxygen, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(62, 62, 64); letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">Let's do a quick review:</p><ul style="margin: 0.7em 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-weight: 300; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Oxygen, Oxygen, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box; list-style: none; color: rgb(62, 62, 64); letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><li>A <strong style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: bold; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Oxygen, Oxygen, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box;">module</strong> contains the different components of an AngularJS appA <strong style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: bold; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Oxygen, Oxygen, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box;">controller</strong> manages the app's dataAn <strong style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: bold; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Oxygen, Oxygen, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box;">expression</strong> displays values on the pageA <strong style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: bold; font-stretch: inherit; font-family: Oxygen, Oxygen, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: break-word; box-sizing: border-box;">filter</strong> formats the value of an expression</li></ul></div><div><b><br/></b></div><hr/><div><b>Object Construction</b></div><div><p style="margin: 0px 0px 18px; font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, &quot;Hevetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 15px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); box-sizing: border-box; -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><strong style="font-weight: bold; box-sizing: border-box; -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0);">Literal Notation</strong>, where we use</p><pre style="box-sizing: border-box; -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-color: rgb(35, 44, 49); color: rgb(197, 200, 198); border-radius: 2px; overflow: auto; padding: 7px 10px; font-size: 15px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;"><code style="box-sizing: border-box; -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); color: rgb(197, 200, 198); font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, Consolas, source-code-pro, monospace; font-size: 0.85em; padding: 0px; border-radius: 2px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.0470588); border: 1px solid rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.0666667);"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); color: rgb(178, 148, 187);">var</span> Name = { };
</code></pre><div style="margin: 0px 0px 18px; box-sizing: border-box; -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><div><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><span style="font-family: 'Open Sans', 'Hevetica Neue', Helvetica, sans-serif;"><strong style="font-weight: bold; box-sizing: border-box; -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0);">Constructor Notation</strong>, where we use the keyword </span><code style="box-sizing: border-box; -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); padding: 0.15em 0.25em; font-size: 0.85em; border-radius: 2px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.0470588); border: 1px solid rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.0666667); font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, Consolas, source-code-pro, monospace;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0);">new</span></code><span style="font-family: 'Open Sans', 'Hevetica Neue', Helvetica, sans-serif;">.</span></span></div><div><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><span style="font-family: 'Open Sans', 'Hevetica Neue', Helvetica, sans-serif;"><br/></span></span></div><div><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"> </span><ul style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; list-style: none; box-sizing: border-box; -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, &quot;Hevetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 15px; font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><li style="box-sizing: border-box; -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); margin-top: 9px; margin-bottom: 9px;"><strong style="font-weight: bold; box-sizing: border-box; -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0);">Literal notation</strong> creates a single object. Literal notation uses curly brackets <code style="box-sizing: border-box; -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); padding: 0.15em 0.25em; font-size: 0.85em; border-radius: 2px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.0470588); border: 1px solid rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.0666667); font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, Consolas, source-code-pro, monospace;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0);">{ <span style="box-sizing: border-box; -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0);">}</span></span></code> and the object's default properties are defined within the brackets using <code style="box-sizing: border-box; -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); padding: 0.15em 0.25em; font-size: 0.85em; border-radius: 2px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.0470588); border: 1px solid rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.0666667); font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, Consolas, source-code-pro, monospace;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0);">property</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box; -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0);">:value</span></code>notation.</li><li style="box-sizing: border-box; -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); margin-top: 9px; margin-bottom: 9px;"><strong style="font-weight: bold; box-sizing: border-box; -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0);">Constructor notation</strong> involves defining an object <em style="font-style: italic; box-sizing: border-box; -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0);">constructor</em>. And like defining a function, we use the <code style="box-sizing: border-box; -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); padding: 0.15em 0.25em; font-size: 0.85em; border-radius: 2px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.0470588); border: 1px solid rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.0666667); font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, Consolas, source-code-pro, monospace;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0);">function</span></code> keyword. You can think of this constructor as a &quot;template&quot; from which you can create multiple objects. To create a new object from a constructor, we use the <code style="box-sizing: border-box; -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); padding: 0.15em 0.25em; font-size: 0.85em; border-radius: 2px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.0470588); border: 1px solid rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.0666667); font-family: Monaco, Menlo, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, Consolas, source-code-pro, monospace;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box; -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0);">new</span></code> keyword.</li></ul></div></div></div><hr/><div><b>A Web Server Gateway Interface (WSGI)</b></div><div>server implements the web server side of the WSGI interface for running Python web applications. ... Why use WSGI and not just point a web server directly at an application? ... WSGI servers handle processing requests from the web server and deciding ...</div><div><br/></div><div><b>Border Gateway Protocol (BGP)</b></div><div>is a routing protocol used to transfer data and information between different host gateways, the Internet or autonomous systems. BGP is a Path Vector Protocol (PVP), which maintains paths to different hosts, networks and gateway routers and determines the routing decision based on that.</div><div><br/></div><hr/><div><b>What is Jank?</b></div><div>Modern browsers try to refresh the content on screen in sync with a device's refresh rate. For most devices today, the screen will refresh 60 times a second, or 60Hz. If there is some motion on screen (such as scrolling, transitions, or animations) a browser should create 60 frames per second to match the refresh rate.</div><div><br/></div><div>Jank is any stuttering, juddering or just plain halting that users see when a site or app isn't keeping up with the refresh rate. Jank is the result of frames taking too long for a browser to make, and it negatively impacts your users and how they experience your site or app.</div><div><b><br/></b></div><table style="box-sizing: inherit; border: 0px; border-collapse: collapse; border-spacing: 0px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 14px; font-family: Roboto, sans-serif; margin: 0px;
